Chapter 301: Reincarnated Incarnation

Qin Yanyan finally understood why her father had always been reluctant to reveal his identity.

Although Qin Haoran was the leader of one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds and a hegemon of the dark world, commanding countless ruthless and bloodthirsty diabolic cultivators who wouldn’t even blink at slaughter, he couldn’t flaunt such an identity.

Otherwise, if Qin Yanyan ran into an enemy who boasted about hailing from some top-tier sect, demanding, “You better admit defeat,” she might flash a devilish smile and announce that her father was a diabolic creed leader, responding, “You better surrender lest this young miss beats you to death.” After that, her opponent would simply have to report her to the authorities, and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed would be wiped out and flattened.

The end.

The leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was the number one wanted criminal in the Great Xia Dynasty. It would be equivalent to walking right into a trap.

Moreover, if Qin Yanyan’s identity were exposed, everyone would learn that her father was a diabolic creed leader, jeopardizing her political vetting and future prospects.

Most importantly, Qin Haoran had incurred massive debts, making his life unstable, with the constant risk of debt collectors chasing him down. If Su Yiren were to find out about all this, she might decide that Qin Haoran was unreliable and divorce him.

“Are you really sure you don’t remember where the treasure was hidden?” Meng Jingzhou was unwilling to give up. After all, this is the treasure of a diabolic creed leader. Its value is immeasurable. freewebnovel.com

Li Haoran furrowed his brows, trying hard to recall the memories from that time. Qin Haoran’s memory fragments were disjointed and blurry in places, akin to looking at flowers in the fog. “Let me think, let me think...it should be from four hundred years ago...related to the locust trees...”

Lu Yang pondered for a moment and sent an auditory message to the three female ghosts.

~~~

In the main hall, the sound of reading echoed through the air, infusing the rundown temple with a fresh vitality. The three scantily clad female ghosts moved about the hall, stirring excitement among the scholars.

“Whoever performs well in this class will receive private lessons from me,” the green-robed female ghost purred softly, her voice dripping with a bewitching charm.

The scholars’ eyes lit up, and they began to study with unprecedented enthusiasm. “To study and practice regularly, is that not a pleasure...”[1]

Upon hearing Lu Yang’s auditory message, the three female ghosts clapped their hands and announced, “The teachers have something to attend to. The next class will be self-study.” With that, they left the befuddled scholars behind and headed to the side room.

~~~

“How many locust trees in Guhuai Town are over four hundred years old?”

The three female ghosts were taken aback by the question, but Little Seven, the cleverest among them, answered, “There are currently eighty locust trees over four hundred years old, though not all the trees from four centuries ago have survived to this day. Some were cut down to craft furniture, while others were burned as firewood. In fact, there was a conflagration in Guhuai Town that burned down entire groves of locust trees.”

Meng Jingzhou felt that the situation was more complicated than he had thought. Initially, he had assumed that there wouldn’t be many locust trees over four hundred years old, which meant they could investigate them one by one. But it turned out that most of the trees hadn’t survived until now.

Lu Yang nodded. “When do you hand over the yang energy to Lord Mi?”

“Early tomorrow morning.”

“What is Lord Mi’s cultivation realm?”

“He should be at the Basic Nascent Soul Stage.”

This was roughly what Lu Yang had guessed. In diabolic creeds, those in charge at the commandery level were largely at the Basic Nascent Soul Stage. Those like Branch Leader Chu of Yanjiang Commandery, who was only at the Advanced Golden Core Stage, were in the minority. After all, the cultivation levels of cultivators in Yanjiang Commandery were generally low, so there was no need to appoint someone with a higher cultivation level to oversee the region.

“Tomorrow, the three of you will follow my instructions...”

~~~

In a basement in Shoutian Commandery that cost twenty spirit stones a month, Lord Mi, the person-in-charge of Shoutian Commandery for the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, was gingerly pouring tea for a handsome young man.

The young man’s cultivation wasn’t high; he was at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

“Lord Mi, you’re too polite. I’m just a bottom-level member in the creed. I wouldn’t dare trouble you.”

“Please, I’m not worthy to be called Lord Mi. Sir Qin, just call me Old Mi.”

Lord Mi smiled obsequiously while cursing inwardly. Who would dare treat you as a bottom-level follower?

The young man sipped his tea leisurely, displaying no respect for Lord Mi, as if the latter was his subordinate. “You should be clear about the purpose of my visit, Lord Mi.”

“Is it for the treasure that Creed Leader Qin hid in Guhuai Town?”

The young man put down his teacup and spoke with conviction. “To be precise, it’s for my treasure.”

Seeing Lord Mi hesitate, the young man crossed his arms and leaned back in his chair. “What, do you still not believe that I am Qin Haoran’s reincarnation, Lord Mi?”

“You jest, Sir Qin. Everyone in the sect knows you are Creed Leader Qin’s reincarnation.” That said, Lord Mi thought otherwise.

At some point, a rumor had spread within the creed that the previous creed leader, Qin Haoran, had managed to glimpse part of the true meaning of reincarnation. Although his life tablet had shattered and he had seemingly perished, he had actually entered the cycle of reincarnation to prepare for the Battle of the Great Era.

Recently, three young men surnamed Qin had appeared, each claiming to be Qin Haoran’s reincarnation and seeking to inherit his bequest. All three were supported by high-ranking members of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, so no one dared to openly claim that these young men were not Qin Haoran's reincarnations, nor could anyone assert which one of them was the true reincarnation.

This involved a power struggle among the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s higher-ups.

Lord Mi suspected that the higher-ups had split into three factions, each wanting to seize Qin Haoran’s legacy. Thus, they had pushed forward their respective representatives of “Qin Haoran’s incarnation.”

The young man before him was one of the three suspected incarnations. This was why Lord Mi treated him with such deference, not daring to slight him.

What if he really is Creed Leader Qin’s reincarnation?

It doesn’t hurt to be polite. And surely someone like him would travel with protectors, right? They must be hiding in the shadows, ensuring this young man’s safety.

Lord Mi speculated that the young man’s situation was unstable and wanted to strengthen his claim as Qin Haoran’s reincarnation by locating the treasure Qin Haoran had left in Guhuai Town.

The rumors surrounding the treasure in Guhuai Town were diverse. This wasn’t something Qin Haoran had voluntarily told the masses. Instead, it was one of his close confidants who had revealed the matter after his death.

This confidant said that Creed Leader Qin had placed some papers in a wooden box. From the corner of his eye, he noticed that the papers had large sums of spirit stones written, suggesting they were banknotes that could be exchanged for spirit stones at merchant guilds. From the tiny clues left by Creed Leader Qin, the confidant deduced that Creed Leader Qin had hidden the wooden box in Guhuai Town.

At first, the confidant didn’t pay much attention to this, but after Qin Haoran passed away, covetous intentions brewed within him, and he wanted to claim the wooden box for himself. However, Qin Haoran had placed a special seal on the wooden box to block all external probing methods.

Even when the higher-ups learned of this, they failed to find the wooden box. They also didn’t dare to turn Guhuai Town upside down in a blatant search, fearing it would alert the imperial court. Therefore, the matter was put on hold, with Lord Mi keeping an eye on it.

Despite keeping watch for several years, Lord Mi gained nothing. He simply asked the female ghosts about it every time to prove to the higher-ups that he was still diligently pursuing the search.

1. This is from Lunyu or The Analects of Confucius. In fact, it’s the opening line. I found a post comparing a few English translations, so feel free to check it out to gain different perspectives. ☜

Chapter 302: Geniuses Who Have Slumbered Since Ancient Times

“Sir Qin, may I ask how you plan to find your treasure?”

Sir Qin chuckled softly. “Lord Mi, why do you think I chose to hide my treasure in Guhuai Town? Was it random? No, no. What do you think Guhuai Town is most famous for?”

Lord Mi hesitated. “Female ghosts?” He was reminded of the three female ghosts with the highest performance.

Lord Mi planned to have the three female ghosts summarize their experiences and report them to him. He would then present these as successful case studies to the higher-ups to promote sustainable yang energy absorption strategies, improve living conditions for the female ghosts in the creed, and increase the efficiency of yang energy absorption.

What Little Seven and the other two ghosts didn’t know was that Lord Mi had hundreds of ghosts under his command, all assiduously gathering yang energy. But only the three of them were top performers, earning Lord Mi’s favor.

Sir Qin, “...”

He suppressed his anger and forced a smile. “It’s the locust trees.

“Locust trees nurture ghosts and are rare conduits between the yin and yang realms. Our creed believes in the existence of the Nine Netherworlds, and the locust trees align with our creed’s teachings.

“In my past life, I was well-versed in this and fond of locust trees. Guhuai Town, with its abundance of locust trees, naturally caught my attention back then.

“Hence, the past me buried the treasure beneath a locust tree and sealed it with multiple layers of protection. Along with the effect of the yin energy from the ancient locust trees, the treasure would be obscured from detection methods such as spiritual consciousness, karma, and heavenly eyes. Only the naked eye of those in the living realm can find it.” Sir Qin spoke with an air of serenity, as if he was reminiscing about the experiences in his past life.

In truth, he didn't know where Qin Haoran had hidden the treasure. However, he had the backing of a higher-up in the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, who was proficient in the ways of karma and had paid a price to roughly calculate the clues to Qin Haoran’s treasure.

Locust trees.

This was the result of that higher-up’s calculations.

With this lead, he simply needed to methodically search Guhuai Town for a while, believing he would eventually find it.

As for Lord Mi, he had been observing all this time, so he was the perfect witness.

This way, my identity as the reincarnation of Creed Leader Qin will be cemented.

“Unfortunately, the matter of reincarnation is too complex and entangles far too much. Even though I successfully reincarnated, I still cannot fully comprehend the mysteries of the cycle of reincarnation. At the moment, I have only unlocked a corner of my past life’s memories and cannot recall the exact location of the treasure.” Sir Qin shook his head, his tone laced with melancholy and regret.

“In that case, I will go to Guhuai Town tomorrow to collect the yang energy. Would you like to accompany me, Sir Qin?”

“Very well.”

~~~

Early the next morning, Lord Mi brought Sir Qin to the worn-down temple in Guhuai Town.

Sir Qin subconsciously frowned, somewhat disdainful of the shabby temple. “Here?”

Lord Mi smiled. “Sir Qin, don’t underestimate this place. It provides a large amount of yang energy every month. Just Guhuai Town alone can collect as much yang energy as seven or eight towns, sometimes even more.”

“That is interesting. I’d like to hear more.”

“There are three female ghosts here. They have forgotten their past lives and real names, so they gave themselves nicknames: Little Five, Little Six, and Little Seven. Little Seven is the youngest and the most intelligent and has the highest cultivation talent among the three sisters, with her cultivation at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. Her two older sisters are at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage.”

Sir Qin was rather astonished. Logically, a place as small as Guhuai Town shouldn’t be able to nurture a ghost at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. I can only say that this ghost called Little Seven does have some abilities.

“Little Five, Little Six, Little Seven, come out!” Lord Mi ordered the three female ghosts to appear.

The three female ghosts floated out of the temple, timidly calling out, “Lord Mi,” their voices tickling the hearts of those who heard them.

Each of them held a mutton fat jade[1] bottle containing the yang energy they had collected over the past month.

Sir Qin’s spirits lifted. He had seen many female cultivators and ghosts with decent looks, but he had never encountered anyone like these three female ghosts, especially Little Seven.

When Little Seven and the others saw Sir Qin, they were surprised. Lord Mi always came alone; why has he brought someone today?

Sir Qin is not included in our plan.

“Lord Mi, can you lend me these three female ghosts? They have been wandering Guhuai Town for a long time and can be of great help in my search for the treasure.” Sir Qin’s selfish desires were stirred.

“Rest assured, Lord Mi. I know they are your money-making trees.[2] I just want to borrow them for a short while. Once I find the treasure, I’ll return them to you. How’s that?”

Lord Mi was hesitant. I’m certainly not willing, but this person is suspected to be Creed Leader Qin’s reincarnation. If I offend him, he’ll definitely make life difficult for me in the future.

He gritted his teeth. It isn’t worth offending Creed Leader Qin’s reincarnation over three female ghosts. “Fine, I’ll lend them to you then, Sir Qin.”

Lord Mi formed a hand seal, preparing to transfer the soul restriction to Sir Qin, when suddenly, his expression changed. He pulled the dazed Sir Qin away, hastily retreating.

Three sword qi descended from the sky, piercing the spot where Lord Mi had just been standing. The sword qi was sharp, slicing through the soil like tofu. After plunging into the ground, it was unclear how many meters it penetrated before finally disappearing.

Lord Mi was shaken. The three sword qi had been aimed at his vital points. If not for his unique cultivation technique, which allowed him to evade danger to some degree, he would have been forced to use the life-saving magical treasure he had obtained at the cost of his fortune to block the attack.

Clap, clap, clap.

Nonchalant applause came from behind the three female ghosts, sounding like a frivolous young master.

“What impressive skills, Lord Mi. I thought those three sword strikes would at least cause you some trouble even if they couldn’t kill you. I didn’t expect you to be so agile and dodge them in advance.”

As the dust dissipated, four youthful figures appeared—three men and one woman—all full of vitality and exceptional talent. Compared to them, even Sir Qin, who was suspected to be the creed leader’s reincarnation, seemed to pale in comparison in their presence.

“Who are you?!” Lord Mi was on high alert. They know my identity and have clearly come prepared; they’re not afraid of my Nascent Soul cultivation.

Most importantly, two are at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, and two are at the Basic Golden Core Stage. The sword qi was likely unleashed by one of the Basic Golden Core cultivators.

But how could sword qi from a Basic Golden Core cultivator have posed a threat to me?

What kind of genius is this?

Not even S-Class sects can produce such talent; only the Five Great Immortal Sects can groom such a peerless prodigy. Or maybe it’s because the Great Xia Dynasty intends to nurture a potential candidate for the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?

Regardless of which case it is, the situation is dire.

“Five Great Immortal Sects? Imperial court?” Lord Mi prepared himself. If the situation took even the slightest turn for the worse, he would flee immediately.

The person who had just clapped was the leader of the four. He seemed unaware of Lord Mi’s vigilance and hostility as he chatted with him jovially. “You’re Lord Mi of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, right?”

He picked at his fingernails, not even looking up. “My name is Lu Yiyang.”[3]

Without warning, Lu Yang looked up, his eyes blazing with intensity like twin swords, causing Lord Mi to flinch and avoid his gaze in fear.

Lord Mi instinctively blinked, but he couldn’t discern anything unusual; it felt as if he had just experienced a hallucination.

“Lord Mi, you’re not very well-informed, so you probably haven’t heard of us.”

Lu Yang chuckled. “The Five Great Immortal Sects? The Great Xia Dynasty? What are they?

“We were all geniuses from ancient times with the aspiration of becoming immortals. Unfortunately, back then, the Heaven Mandate Immortal and others were envious of our talents and set up obstacles, blocking the path to immortal ascension. Thus, we had no choice but to enter a deep slumber, choosing to awaken before the Great Era to compete for the immortal’s Dao Fruit and restore the glory of our Heavenly Court.”

1. It’s a type of premium-grade white jade. You would likely have come across this in Chinese novels because it’s one of the top standards for white jade. ☜

2. The yaoqianshu term here is a legendary tree that would drop money when shaken. ☜

3. The “yi” here is the character for the number “one.” ☜

Chapter 303: Heavenly Court Creed

Geniuses from ancient times?!

The Heaven Mandate Immortal was envious of their talents?!

Lord Mi was deeply shaken by these two bombshell revelations.

As the Great Era approached, many experts from the past were awakening. Some were from the Great Yu Dynasty, while others were from the Great Qian Dynasty. However, they had one thing in common—their minimal cultivation was the Advanced Fusion Stage, with foundations so solid it was terrifying. They were qualified to step onto the stage of the Great Era and vie for the fortuitous opportunity to ascend to an immortal.

But I haven’t heard any news of cultivators from the ancient era awakening.

Yet, the cultivation realm and combat power of these individuals are undeniable. A Golden Core cultivator going against the tide to fight a Nascent Soul cultivator? Such geniuses can be counted on one hand and deserve to leave their names in history.

Judging by their tone, the Five Great Immortal Sects and the Great Xia Dynasty seem to be nothing in their eyes. And it didn’t sound like they were faking it either.

Is it true or false?

The more I think about it, the more frightening it becomes. If it were true, that would be absolutely horrifying. This is definitely not something a mere Nascent Soul cultivator like me should get involved in.

Hold on. Lord Mi sensed something off. The sword qi from earlier might not have been unleashed by them. It’s likely that they used a sword qi talisman given by an elder.

“Drop the mysterious act!” Lord Mi felt that he had seen through their facade. A surge of black energy rose from his chest, and a Knife-Wielding Ghost[1] emerged, merging with Lord Mi.

His aura changed in an instant. Wielding a bone-cleaving knife, he was like a ghostly general. I have to capture these four youngsters in one fell swoop and show them that I’m not so easily fooled.

This was an extremely obscure cultivation method known as the Five Organs Ghost Commanding Technique, where one nurtured five ghosts within their five organs. During battle, the ghosts could either possess the host’s body or be commanded by them, allowing for both close and ranged combat.

One of the figures behind Lu Yang narrowed his eyes and brazenly attacked with full explosive power. His brilliance was like the sun, subduing all demons and monsters and suppressing all evil.

Bang!

The two forces collided with a deafening roar, sending tremors through the earth.

“Long Jingzhou, I’ll leave it to you.”

Meng Jingzhou couldn’t stop his peals of laughter as he looked down at Lord Mi. “A bunch of evil creed followers who don’t even know the origins of the Nine Netherworlds dare to attack me?”

His body ignited with raging flames, causing the surroundings to boil, as if a sun had risen from the ground.

The ghost possessing Lord Mi let out a blood-curdling scream, its body continuously melting away.

This was the Pure Yang True Fire that every cultivator with a Single’s Spirit Root would obtain. It was the ultimate yang energy—the bane of all ghosts and monsters.

Just a glance at the Pure Yang True Fire was sufficient to make Sir Qin feel as though his eyes were burning. He had to use all his cultivation to suppress the sensation.

Anyone else fighting Lord Mi for the first time would be unaccustomed to his ghost-commanding combat style, putting them at a disadvantage. Unfortunately for Lord Mi, he had encountered Meng Jingzhou, a cultivator who dared to form two Single Golden Cores, resulting in Meng Jingzhou’s Pure Yang True Fire being the strongest among all Single’s Spirit Root cultivators in history.

Ghost energy spiraled around Lord Mi, creating quite a scary sight. But in reality, this was a sign of his ghost energy leaking out everywhere; he was already at a disadvantage.

Meng Jingzhou’s iron fists slammed into the knife, leaving countless fist imprints on its surface.

“That’s enough,” Lu Yang said insipidly.

Meng Jingzhou tactfully stepped back, sparing Lord Mi’s life.

Lord Mi was still in disarray. He quickly recalled the Knife-Wielding Ghost back into his heart to recuperate; it wouldn’t be able to fight again for a while.

This time, Lord Mi was certain that the people he was dealing with were truly peerless geniuses. A Basic Golden Core cultivator could corner a Basic Nascent Soul cultivator like me into a disadvantage. Although I didn’t expend all my methods, did they necessarily display their full strength?

They look so relaxed as if they hadn’t even fought at all.

Whether they drew the envy of the Heaven Mandate Immortal, I don’t know. But I can be certain that even in this era of abundant geniuses, there are no more than ten with such talent!

“Lord Mi, we are actually not enemies. While it’s true that the Five Great Immortal Sects and the Great Xia Dynasty are so fragile they crumble in a single blow, our Heavenly Court Creed has yet to fully awaken, so we lack the strength to confront them in their entirety.

“Moreover, we have a deep-seated enmity with the Dao-Seeking Sect!

“The Dao-Seeking Sect single-handedly destroyed the Everlasting Creed and cut off any chance of the Everlasting Immortal’s resurrection. The Everlasting Immortal was the protector of our ancient Heavenly Court and holds immense significance to us!” Hatred and killing intent toward the Dao-Seeking Sect flickered in Lu Yang’s eyes.

“Heavenly Court?” Lord Mi revealed a perplexed expression. They keep mentioning “Heavenly Court.”

What is the Heavenly Court? Why haven’t I heard of it before?

Lu Yang patiently explained, “The Heavenly Court was the ruler of the ancient era. The stars in the sky, the cycles of nature—all were under the jurisdiction of our Heavenly Court.

“In the age before the rise of the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others, all living beings revered the Heavenly Court. Unfortunately, as the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the rest rose to power, the Heavenly Court’s dominance waned, and we gradually fell into decline.

“The Heavenly Court worshipped the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign—Dou Heavenly Sovereign. Even the most resplendent stars were but a mere insignificant yellow soybean in the presence of the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign.

“Dou Heavenly Sovereign was the first in the world to ascend to an immortal. However, that abhorrent Nine-Layers Immortal concealed the existence of the Heavenly Court by stealing the glory of the Dou Heavenly Sovereign and claiming to be the first to ascend!”[2]

Lord Mi was flabbergasted. He didn’t even know about the Nine-Layers Immortal, let alone that they were the first to become an immortal. From Lu Yang’s short speech, he caught a whiff of the brutal struggles of ancient times. It seems that the ancient era was filled with deceit and treachery, and immortals were no exception!

Lu Yang continued, “We are all members of the Heavenly Court who have awakened from our deep slumber. We wish to build the Heavenly Court Creed and leverage the arrival of the Great Era to restore the former glory of the Heavenly Court!

“The few of us are not the only ones who have awakened from the ancient era. Some elders are lying low in various places, quietly waiting for more elders to awaken and plot our grand scheme.”

Lord Mi wondered, Could it be that no ancient cultivators have awakened until now, not because there are none in slumber but because all of them were members of the Heavenly Court Creed? And after awakening, they have all hidden themselves? It makes sense that the ancient concealment methods were unknown to the Great Xia Dynasty.

Behind Sir Qin was a Divine Transfiguration cultivator in hiding, sent by the higher-ups of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed to protect Sir Qin. He hadn’t expected to encounter such a situation.

Just as he was about to reveal himself and rebuke Lu Yang for spouting nonsense, Lu Yang suddenly raised his eyes and met his gaze.

How is this possible? My concealment technique is rare in the world. How could he have discovered me, especially since he’s only at the Basic Golden Core Stage?!

Unless there’s also a protector hidden nearby whose cultivation is far above mine?!

The Divine Transfiguration cultivator soon realized this possibility and dared not make any further moves.

Lu Yang withdrew his gaze. It was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy who had informed him that a Divine Transfiguration cultivator was hiding behind Sir Qin.

Fortunately, I had scared him off with just a gaze.

A smart person would automatically fill in the blanks about why I had discovered him—that’d save me the hassle.

“The relationship between the Heavenly Court Creed and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed is closer than you imagine, Lord Mi. The Heavenly Court represents the heavens, embodying yang attributes and governing the yang realm, the world of the living. The Nine Netherworlds represent the earth, embodying yin attributes and governing the yin realm, the underworld. Both the Heavenly Court and the Nine Netherworlds were the true rulers of the primordial ancient era!”

“What?!” Lord Mi exclaimed, never imagining that the Nine Netherworlds and the Heavenly Court were this closely related.

It was not only Lord Mi; even the Divine Transfiguration cultivator hiding behind Sir Qin felt his heart tighten. So the Nine Netherworlds originated from the ancient era?

Seeing Lord Mi so flustered, Lu Yang gently shook his head, as if he was deeply pained by their reaction.

“It looks like with the end of the distant ancient era, many legacies have been lost. Even the most ancient Nine Netherworlds have completely forgotten their relationship with the Heavenly Court.

“That’s why we said earlier that there’s no need for us to fight to the death. Lord Mi, think about it. If we were from the Five Great Immortal Sects or the Great Xia Dynasty, why wouldn’t we have wiped you all out by now instead of wasting time here talking?

“If you still don’t believe us, we have more evidence.

“In the ancient era, the Heavenly Court and the Nine Netherworlds were on good terms. Our elders knew some reincarnation spells, and using these spells, we found the reincarnation of your previous creed leader, Qin Haoran!”

1. Caoguidao is the nickname of Cao Zheng, a character in the classic novel Shui Hu Zhuan or Water Margin. I tried to follow the most common English translation of his title, but I did tweak it a little. ☜

2. I hope I made it obvious, but if it isn’t, they’re talking about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou here. ☜

Chapter 304: Duped Beyond Recovery

Despite initially appearing indifferent, Sir Qin’s expression shifted upon hearing Lu Yang’s words. Whether Lu Yang was an ancient genius or a member of the Heavenly Court Creed has nothing to do with him, nor is it something I have the right to interfere with.

But Lu Yang claims that he has found Qin Haoran’s reincarnation? That won’t do.

If they’ve found Qin Haoran’s reincarnation, what would that make me?

Sir Qin had a clear understanding of himself—the purpose of his existence was to rightfully inherit Qin Haoran’s bequest.

Even if he was the same age as Lu Yang and the others, he was already at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, his progress in cultivation faster than Lu Yang’s junior disciples.

In reality, his cultivation was far from as impressive as it seemed. The higher-ups of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed had forcibly elevated his cultivation to make him appear as talented as Qin Haoran.

However, this was akin to helping seedlings grow by pulling them upward, resulting in dire consequences. His future cultivation would be fraught with hardships, and advancement to the Fusion Stage would be as difficult as climbing to the heavens; he might be stuck at the Void Refinement Stage, or even lower, for his whole life.

“Who did you say is this esteemed one’s reincarnation?” Sir Qin boomed as his gaze bore into Lu Yang, looking like he wished he could devour him in one bite.

Qin Haoran was most proficient in arrays; coincidentally, Qin Tian was also adept in arrays.

Chapter 305: I Became My Dad’s Reincarnation?

Chapter 306: The Item Qin Haoran Hid

Qin Yanyan had just stepped into human society, and she was already struck by how profound, unfathomable, and unpredictable it was.

Lu Yang had thought that his plan was quite thorough. First, he would leverage his extensive knowledge of the ancient era to weave a grand narrative, constructing an imaginary Heavenly Court Creed and conferring upon Huang Doudou the title of Dou Heavenly Sovereign.

I, Shi Huagu, hereby establish this written pledge, acknowledging that I owe one billion spirit stones. Should I fail to repay within the stipulated time, may the heavens strike me with five thunderbolts.

1. The name sounds somewhat ominous because if you combine “shi” and “hua,” you get “petrify into stone,” and if you combine “hua” and “gu,” which is his name, it means something like “turning into bones” or “dissolving bones.” ☜

Chapter 307: Unlucky Vice Creed Leader

~~~

At the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s headquarters, stormy clouds loomed low, and a once-in-a-century lightning tribulation brewed in the sky.

Even nine lives won’t be enough then.

“What?” Shi Huagu thought his brain had been fried by the lightning.

“Ah, no, it’s nothing. I meant to say, ah, it’s the Heavenly Court,” the creed leader quickly corrected himself.

After becoming the creed leader and seeing the monthly deficit reports, he finally realized how difficult life had been for the previous creed leader.

He strived to lead the Nine-Netherworlds Creed to greater heights. For the sake of their faith, he studied finance from scratch and conducted market research and field investigations. Identifying business opportunities from the small details, he set up various new industries and worked assiduously to earn money to keep the Nine-Netherworlds Creed afloat.

Unfortunately, no matter how many spirit stones he earned, it was never sufficient to fill the bottomless pit of building the Fengdu Ghost City.[1]

However, he couldn’t reveal this to anyone, for it would easily cause panic among the members. Facing suppression from the righteous path was already stressful. If the followers learned about the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s dire situation, they might even consider turning themselves in.

Thus, he greatly admired Qin Haoran. Despite such a huge deficit, he could still maintain the creed’s daily operations.

If he were to find out that Qin Haoran managed to start a family and build a career under such circumstances, he would probably admire him even more.

“Qin Haoran’s reincarnation...”

Previously, he had thought that Qin Haoran’s reincarnation was something the three vice creed leaders had fabricated to compete for his legacy. The Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s teachings mentioned “Reincarnation,” which was theoretically possible. However, throughout the creed’s long history, no one had ever heard of anyone achieving reincarnation successfully.

But now, an ancient Heavenly Court Creed has emerged, claiming to have found Qin Haoran’s reincarnation. To top it off, the person is a woman.

Although it sounds strange, upon closer thought, it does make sense.

“Are you sure it belongs to Qin Haoran?”

Shi Huagu silently took out the debt note. He didn’t know about the creed’s financial losses and assumed that Qin Haoran had left the debt note behind to sabotage people.

The moment the creed leader laid his eyes on the debt note, he was confident that it belonged to Qin Haoran. Furthermore, he remembered that Qin Haoran was proficient in karma and arrays, capable of blocking and transferring karma.

“In that case, the credibility of the Heavenly Court Creed and Qin Haoran’s reincarnation is quite high. Call the other two vice creed leaders over for a meeting.”

Shi Huagu didn’t want to be struck by lightning every month. “Can the one billion spirit stones be taken from the treasury?”

The creed leader replied sternly, “Your accepting Qin Haoran’s inheritance is a private matter. You can’t use public funds. There must be a clear distinction between public and private matters!

“But I have a small suggestion.”

“Please go ahead, Creed Leader.”

“Next time you get struck by lightning, please stay further away from the headquarters. Repairing the headquarters costs money.”

1. According to legends, Fengdu is where the ghosts are managed in the underworld. ☜

Chapter 308: The Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s Regular Meeting

At the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s headquarters, a long rectangular conference table occupied the center of the room. The creed leader sat on one side, facing the three vice creed leaders on the other. Beside each seat sat white porcelain teacups filled with steaming water.

The creed leader cleared his throat and opened his notebook. “Let’s begin today’s meeting. There are three items on the agenda. First, Vice Creed Leader Xiang will report on the creed’s activities over the past month.”

Vice Creed Leader Xiang had a peculiar appearance, with three eyes on his forehead that allowed him to keep his eyes on all directions and perceive everything. He was the executive vice creed leader in charge of everyday affairs.

“Since the sixth month, the creed has demonstrated a stable and improving trend. This month, we gained thirty-three new disciples: twenty-three male cultivators, ten female cultivators, and three non-humans—ghosts.

“The proportion of male cultivators remains high. The creed leader’s directive to recruit more female cultivators has not been fully achieved, but we will continue to rectify this and strive to achieve a balanced gender ratio as soon as possible.

“This month, eighteen creed followers were arrested by the Great Xia Dynasty. Three went missing in the Demon Region, and two turned themselves in after being persuaded by the Hanging Monastery.

“According to reliable sources, the Great Xia Dynasty is revising the Great Xia Dynasty Ghost Management Regulations in response to the increasingly severe situation of rampant ghosts. Once these regulations are officially launched, the activities of our creed’s ghosts may be restricted, indirectly affecting the progress of Fengdu Ghost City’s construction.

“In terms of new business ventures, the creed has dutifully embodied the creed leader’s directives and guiding principles, actively promoting diversified entrepreneurial channels. We have rolled out a one-stop funeral and cremation service, encouraging both commoners and cultivators to bury their remains in the cemeteries established by our creed. We also offer tomb rental services, with plans to charge fees every fifty years.

“Our creed has also vigorously developed the smuggling industry, effectively pushing for the implementation of the Great Xia Dynasty Smuggling Laws. The Great Xia Dynasty has encouraged and supported our efforts, even awarding us a commendation banner, but no one in the creed dares to claim it. Currently, the smuggling industry is struggling and has meager profits. We will need to explore new ideas.

“While advancing our tomb-raiding business, we have repeatedly encountered the First Elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect. It is suspected that the Dao-Seeking Sect has obtained some clues about our creed’s tomb-raiding patterns.

“In addition, during a tomb raid, we accidentally unearthed an archaic Fusion cultivator in slumber. After a fierce battle, both sides were eventually arrested by the Great Xia Dynasty.

“Finally, after rigorous and thorough investigations, we have eliminated all communication channels established with the Everlasting Creed. It will be impossible for the Great Xia Dynasty and the Dao-Seeking Sect to contact us through the remnants of the Everlasting Creed.

“That is all.”

After listening to the report, the creed leader secretly sighed. It’s really difficult to manage the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. What is all this mess?!

Earning money is truly hard.

“Old Xiang, how did those eighteen unlucky ones get caught by the imperial court?” another vice creed leader asked curiously. His surname was Shi, and he was a ghost cultivator.

He was once a Buddhist sect disciple. While chanting the Rebirth Requiem for the deceased, he used too much force and ended up liberating his own soul, which left his body. Later, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed found him and recruited him into the creed.

Vice Creed Leader Xiang sighed. “Aside from the ten who were caught after the tomb raid led to a battle with an archaic Fusion cultivator, there were also eight idiots.

“I assigned these eight the task of opening a brothel. After some on-site investigation, they decided that the taxes on brothels were too high. Thus, they brought in dozens of female Shapeshifting Demons from the Demon Region and registered a zoo. That way, the tax rates would be much lower.

“Though they called it a zoo, in reality, its offerings were no different from a brothel’s. Whenever the court conducted an inspection, these people would disguise it as a legitimate zoo.”

“That’s quite clever.” Vice Creed Leader Shi was impressed. These eight people have good ideas.

Vice Creed Leader Xiang said gloomily, “The problem is, ordinary zoos don’t have signs that read ‘Minors Prohibited.’

“To make matters worse, a private school teacher heard about the zoo. Under the pretext of broadening the students’ horizons, he led them there for a visit.

“Then, they truly broadened their horizons.”

Vice Creed Leader Shi, “...”

“Ahem, let’s save the experience exchange for after the meeting. Let’s move on to the second item on the agenda.

“Vice Creed Leader Shi, please report on the progress of Fengdu Ghost City’s construction.”

Vice Creed Leader Shi answered, “Everything is going smoothly. Eighty percent is complete. As long as sufficient funds are secured, the remaining twenty percent can be finished quickly.”

The creed leader heaved a sigh of relief. Finally, it’s nearing completion. To build Fengdu Ghost City, I almost had to sell my underpants.

Unfortunately for him, he wasn’t from the Phoenix Tribe. Otherwise, he might have even considered selling his blood.

Aren’t diabolic creeds supposed to be the local underground hegemons that can strut around flaunting their power? Why is our Nine-Netherworlds Creed in such a sorry state?

Look at the Everlasting Creed, the Radiant Sun Creed, and the Heartless Creed. Is any one of them like us?

The other two vice creed leaders’ eyes lit up in excitement at the news. Fengdu Ghost City is our dream. We are the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. How can we not have a city symbolizing the afterlife?

“How many more spirit stones are needed?”

“3.8 billion.”

The creed leader’s hands trembled. This is going to be the death of me.

Is it too late to step down now?

Seventeen years ago, Qin Haoran’s life tablet shattered, and he suddenly died. The Nine-Netherworlds Creed was plunged into turmoil, with four vice creed leaders vying for the position of creed leader.

The four vice creed leaders were similar in cultivation and influence, making it challenging to determine a victor. At that time, an idea suddenly struck him, and he made a promise: if he became the creed leader, he would build Fengdu Ghost City.

It was this promise that garnered him the support of many Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s followers, and he smoothly became the creed leader.

My damn mouth! Whoever wants to be this damn creed leader, be my guest.

Now, it’s too late for regrets.

Despite Qin Haoran’s reign having lasted eight hundred years, he never managed to build Fengdu Ghost City. Yet, this new creed leader was close to completing it in just seventeen years. Naturally, he had his methods.

He was skilled in transformation techniques. Over the past seventeen years, he had used the identities of every creed member to take out loans. If this were exposed, it wouldn’t just mean the end of my tenure as creed leader—it would mean the end of my life.

“The Everlasting Creed has just been destroyed, and the Great Xia Dynasty and the Five Great Immortal Sects are keeping a close watch on us. For safety’s sake, let’s temporarily halt the construction of Fengdu Ghost City.”

The creed leader’s views received the support of the three vice creed leaders. Although the Four Great Diabolic Creeds couldn’t truly unite due to differing beliefs, they had coexisted for over ten thousand years. The annihilation of one creed left the remaining three gripped by a sense of unease.

The diabolic creeds had survived this long precisely because they always prioritized safety.

“Next, let’s move on to the third and final item on the agenda—regarding Qin Haoran’s reincarnation and the authenticity of the Heavenly Court Creed.”

“Heavenly Court Creed?” Vice Creed Leaders Xiang and Shi exchanged baffled glances. It’s always been the Four Great Diabolic Creeds. When did a Heavenly Court Creed appear? And what does this have to do with Qin Haoran’s reincarnation?

Each of the two had also arranged for a young cultivator to claim to be Qin Haoran’s reincarnation.

“Vice Creed Leader Shi, you know this matter best. I’ll leave it to you to explain it.”

Chapter 309: Multiple Versions of the Heavenly Court

Shi Huagu felt that it was a truly unlucky day for him.

First, he was set up by the long-dead Qin Haoran, who left him with a debt of one billion spirit stones, and because he couldn’t repay it, he got struck by lightning.

Later, due to the matter with the Heavenly Court, he recounted the events to the creed leader.

Now, he had to repeat it all over again.

Maybe I should just write a memoir to save myself the trouble of repeatedly reliving those painful experiences.

The two other vice creed leaders stared at Shi Huagu in trepidation. The thunderstorm earlier had been so loud that it was impossible for them not to have heard it. Why would a Fusion cultivator encounter a lightning tribulation? Could this old fellow Shi Huagu have broken through?

With a grim expression, Shi Huagu narrated the events in Guhuai Town in detail, though the focus wasn’t on Qin Yanyan being Qin Haoran’s reincarnation, but rather on the matter of the Heavenly Court Creed.

“The most powerful organization from the ancient era? The Heavenly Court?”

“The first to ascend to an immortal was Dou Heavenly Sovereign?”

“Stars like yellow soybeans and easily manipulated...what kind of divine power is this?!”

The two vice creed leaders gasped. That man named Lu Yiyang had revealed so many ancient secrets in just a few words.

The first to ascend to an immortal? That’s an extraordinary achievement. This was a big shot who pioneered the path to the Immortal Dao. It wouldn’t be an exaggeration to call this figure the ancestor of immortals.

As the higher-ups of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, they were privy to far more secrets than the average Fusion Cultivator. Yet, even they weren’t aware that the first to ascend was the Nine-Layers Immortal.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal usurped Dou Heavenly Sovereign’s position to become the first immortal?”

“It’s always said that in the ancient era, prodigies were like dragons. They brimmed with heroic spirit and grandeur that could engulf the mountains and rivers, possessing unrivaled strength. Who would have thought that such filth lay hidden from our eyes?!”

Seeing that the two vice creed leaders were gradually absorbing the information, the creed leader slowly said, “Actually, I know a little about the Heavenly Court.”

“Please elaborate, Creed Leader.” The other two vice creed leaders felt that they had broadened their horizons today, attaining the chance to learn so many ancient secrets.

The creed leader was pleased with their eagerness and didn’t keep them in suspense. “I once came across an ancient immortal book written by the Nine-Layers Immortal. I asked someone to translate it, but it was only a rough version with missing characters and sentences. Nonetheless, it was enough to understand the gist of the book’s contents.

“The immortal book mentioned the existence of the ‘Heavenly Court,’ stating that numerous immortals existed in the ancient era. Forming a Dao Fruit and ascending to an immortal was merely the first step to the Immortal Dao. Beyond immortals were sages, beyond sages were gods, and beyond gods were supreme gods. The sheer number of realms was astounding.

“The Heavenly Court was the organization of the supreme divine realm, ruling over all things and principles!”

The two vice creed leaders and Shi Huagu were hearing this for the first time. They subconsciously leaned forward, captivated by these ancient secrets.

“Why does this not seem to match with what Lu Yiyang said? Was he lying?” Shi Huagu frowned.

The creed leader waved his hand. “Let me continue. Later, I found another ancient immortal book written by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. The book was titled Imprisoning Heaven, and its main content described the ancient Heavenly Court.

“It stated that immortals could be divided into Human Immortals, Earthly Immortals, Heavenly Immortals, Golden Immortals, Supreme Golden Immortals, and Genesis Immortals. It also mentioned that the supreme ruler of the Heavenly Court was the Heavenly Emperor, who resided in Lingxiao Throne Hall[1] There were also two sages and three purities,[2] who were actual rulers of the Heavenly Court.

“The descriptions in the book were so immersively detailed that it felt like I was there. For some time, I thought it was a novel written by the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

“But upon further contemplation, it didn’t make sense. Who was the Heaven Mandate Immortal? He was an immortal. How could an immortal have had the leisure to write novels? It defied common sense.”

The three vice creed leaders nodded in unison, agreeing with the creed leader’s reasoning.

“After that, I came across another immortal book, also written by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. It mentioned the Heavenly Court and classified immortals into Tier-One Immortals, Tier-Two Immortals, Tier-Three Immortals, Tier-Four Immortals, and Tier-Five Immortals! The storyline in this book was also vastly different from Imprisoning Heaven!”

The three vice creed leaders were dumbfounded. “How could there be such contradictions?” Was the Heaven Mandate Immortal schizophrenic?

The creed leader shook his head. “Originally, I didn’t know the reason either, and I just couldn’t make head or tail of it. I consulted the scholars who studied the primordial ancient era, but they couldn’t provide an answer either. They only said that there were many contradictory stories from the ancient era that remain unexplained to this day.

“But just now, upon learning of the Heavenly Court Creed’s existence, everything fell in place.”

“What do you mean?”

The creed leader explained earnestly, “In the ancient era, a Heavenly Court did exist, but it wasn’t divided into many levels like the Nine-Layers Immortal and the Heaven Mandate Immortal claimed. Instead, just as Lu Yiyang had said, Dou Heavenly Sovereign ruled the Heavenly Court, and the Nine-Layers Immortal usurped the throne.

“To cover up the truth, the Nine-Layers Immortal and the Heaven Mandate Immortal deliberately fabricated history to mislead later generations.”

They quickly painted an image of what they imagined the ancient era to look like.

Dou Heavenly Sovereign was the first to ascend to an immortal. He established the Heavenly Court and became the ruler of the ancient era. Kind and benevolent at heart, He[3] did not hinder later generations from ascending to immortals, allowing others such as the Nine-Layers Immortal and the Heaven Mandate Immortal to ascend one after another.

Driven by fame, profit, or other motives, the Nine-Layers Immortal and the others rebelled against the Heavenly Court and defeated Dou Heavenly Sovereign. The Heavenly Court fell, and the Nine-Layers Immortal and others replaced them as the rulers of the ancient era.

Fearing that their rule would be viewed as illegitimate, the Nine-Layers Immortals and others cloaked themselves in the guise of the Heavenly Court and fabricated an entirely different version of the Heavenly Court, leaving future generations unsure of what they should believe.

“So that’s how it was!” The four of them could sense a faint excitement pumping through their hearts. Putting their heads together, they felt that they had glimpsed a corner of the profound ancient secrets.

“In that case, can the origins of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed also be traced back to the ancient era?”

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed had always claimed that the Nine Netherworlds had existed throughout time, but there was no evidence. Now, with the Heavenly Court Creed as proof, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed could finally hold its head high.

“Lu Yiyang must have withheld some information from us. That said, most of it should be true. We can try to build a connection with them!

“Moreover, the righteous path has been stepping up their efforts to suppress us. As the pinnacle of power in the ancient era, the Heavenly Court Creed’s foundation must run deep. They are perfectly positioned to withstand the attacks from the righteous path!”

They agreed that they only stood to gain from establishing a connection with the Heavenly Court Creed. They tacitly avoided discussing the matter of Qin Haoran and Qin Yanyan. For the sake of Qin Haoran’s bequest, they could never admit that Qin Yanyan was his reincarnation.

If we admit it, wouldn’t we have to hand Qin Haoran’s bequest over to the Heavenly Court Creed?

Although they still couldn’t open Qin Haoran’s bequest, they could easily imagine how enormous the wealth left behind by a Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation expert and a diabolic creed leader must be.

They absolutely couldn’t give it to the Heavenly Court Creed! Even if they believed Qin Yayan to be Qin Haoran’s reincarnation.

“We should go to Yanjiang Commandery to make contact with them and test their foundation,” the creed leader concluded.

“But why a barbeque shop? Is there any significance to that?”

Shi Huagu analyzed seriously, “Looking back at the history of cooking, the first culinary technique humankind mastered was barbeque. The Heavenly Court Creed might be trying to hint at their long history.

“That makes sense!”

"Trust Old Shi to be the most insightful!”

The three took turns lauding Shi Huagu for his clear thinking. Basking in their compliments, even the pain from being struck by lightning seemed to have abated a little.

1. It was believed that this was where the Jade Emperor met with his officials. ☜

2. The Three Purities or Sanqing are the three highest Taoist deities. ☜

3. They are using “He” to refer to a divine being in their imagination. ☜

Chapter 310: Senior Brother Dai: No Matter What Happens This Time, Nothing Can Surprise Me Anymore

“This is the Dao-Seeking Sect?” Qin Yanyan exclaimed in awe as she stood before the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance.

As one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Dao-Seeking Sect was exceptionally active in the cultivation world. Even a cultivator like Qin Yanyan, who rarely ventured beyond her home, had heard of its fame and heroic deeds—subduing demons, vanquishing evil, and upholding justice. All these feats were enough to demonstrate the Dao-Seeking Sect’s tremendous power. In fact, even her mother, Su Yiren, was full of praise for the Dao-Seeking Sect’s strength, saying it might be the strongest among the Five Great Immortal Sects.

After passing through the Great Sect Defense Array, she could clearly sense the difference from the outside world. The temperature and humidity were artificially regulated to the most comfortable levels, and the concentration of spirit qi had significantly increased to the point it was almost comparable to that of her own home.

And her home only housed two people—her and her mother.

As a Fusion expert, Su Yiren had only managed to elevate the spirit qi concentration of a single mountain to this level. But the Dao-Seeking Sect? It spanned a hundred thousand li, yet the concentration of spirit qi in the air was similar to her home.

This is truly terrifying.

“Is this the foundation accumulated over a hundred and twenty thousand years?”

When the four of them walked through a bamboo forest, the babbling river winding through it rippled. The water gushed upward, forming a river spirit.

“Stand right there! Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, who are you bringing into the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

Holding a golden and a silver axe, the River Spirit stared at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou with hostility.

The River Spirit served as the Dao-Seeking Sect’s line of defense, barring riffraff from setting foot inside. When the two vice creed leaders of the Everlasting Creed had previously entered the Dao-Seeking Sect, the River Spirit hadn’t stopped them due to secret instructions from Yun Zhi. Otherwise, even with Lu Yang leading them, the two vice creed leaders wouldn’t have gotten past the entrance.

“This is Qin Yanyan. She’s Junior Brother Li’s family,” Lu Yang introduced readily.

“Family?” The River Spirit cast a suspicious glance at Qin Yanyan, whose cheeks were slightly flushed, and then at Li Haoran, who had a peculiar expression. “I hold information on all disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Why have I never heard of Li Haoran’s family consisting of someone called Qin Yanyan?”

Li Haoran remarked inwardly, I didn’t know either two months ago.

Lu Yang explained briefly, “It’s like this. You should know that Junior Brother Li has a fiancée.”

The River Spirit nodded.

“Junior Brother Li’s fiancée has a daughter—that’s Qin Yanyan.”

The River Spirit was dumbstruck.

When Meng Jingzhou heard the River Spirit say it had information on all the Dao-Seeking Sect’s disciples, his eyes lit up, and he blurted out, “Then you must know Big Senior Sister’s age...”

Suddenly, Lu Yang’s instincts flared. With lightning reflexes, he sent Meng Jingzhou flying with a kick, cutting off his question.

If you want to die, don’t drag everyone down with you!

“Li Haoran, is he telling the truth?” Based on experience, the River Spirit couldn’t fully trust Lu Yang.

Li Haoran hesitantly nodded. “It’s the truth.”

The River Spirit immediately showed Li Haoran respect and allowed the four to pass. “Go ahead. You know the sect’s rules; some areas are off-limits without permission.”

~~~

The first place the four arrived at was the Great Mission Hall. After all, their initial reason for leaving the sect was to complete a mission. Although they encountered some unforeseen circumstances along the way, the mission was ultimately considered done.

“Niece, wait at the entrance. The Great Mission Hall is special. Without permission from an elder-level figure, you can’t enter,” Lu Yang said apologetically to Qin Yanyan.

Qin Yanyan waited at the entrance. As a new face, passing disciples subconsciously glanced at her. Being naturally shy, she couldn’t bear such torture, and her toes were practically digging holes in the ground.

Without warning, two figures caught her attention.

“I heard the River Spirit say that Senior Brother Lu has come to the Great Mission Hall. Let’s go find him for some guidance!”

“Senior Sister Tao, there’s no need to be in such a rush, right? If we wait at the entrance of Heaven’s Gate Peak, we’ll eventually run into Brother Lu.”

A man and a woman chatted as they walked toward the Great Mission Hall.

“Oh, a new face.” The woman noticed Qin Yanyan and warmly greeted her, though the latter was so awkward that she didn’t know where to put her hands and feet.

“I’m Tao Yaoye, and this is Man Gu. Who are you?”

~~~

“Senior Brother, we’re here to report on our mission,” Lu Yang said to the senior male disciple on duty at the front desk.

“The female ghost mission in Guhuai Town, right? Hold on a moment.” Behind the male disciple were stacks of files. He turned around and skillfully pulled out a thin file from the very bottom.

Strangely, even though he had pulled out the bottom file, the mountain-like stack above did not budge an inch.

Lu Yang keenly observed that the files weren’t stacked atop each other but were instead suspended in the air; they were simply clustered so tightly that they appeared to be piled together.

He submitted a detailed account of the incident, Town Mayor Fan’s attestation, and the non-threatening assessment of the female ghosts.

The senior male disciple was knowledgeable. Although using female ghosts as a gimmick to boost local economic development might sound outrageous, according to him, Town Mayor Fan wasn’t the first to do so. However, such matters couldn’t be widely publicized, so they remained mostly unknown.

“Junior Brother Lu, regarding your request to register the three female ghosts with the Dao-Seeking Sect, someone will be sent to conduct an on-site investigation later.”

Though the Dao-Seeking Sect subdued demons and vanquished evil, that didn’t mean they killed every demon, monster, or ghost they encountered. When it came to those who hadn’t harmed people, the Dao-Seeking Sect would file their registration after ensuring they had no history or risk of causing harm to people. This would prevent them from suffering at the hands of misguided righteous cultivators.

If a righteous cultivator insisted on eliminating Little Seven and the others, these three ghosts would only need to present the Dao-Seeking Sect’s registration proof, and the other party would wisely back off.

“In your report, you also mentioned that the three female ghosts were absorbing yang energy under someone’s orders. What’s that about?”

“This matter is related to diabolic creeds. I’ll need to report it to Senior Brother Dai,” Lu Yang replied solemnly.

“Wait a moment, let me inform him.”

~~~

“Lu Yang and the others want to report to me again?” At the moment, Dai Bufan’s body had shrunk and was enveloped by a massive orb of water. He was not the only one inside; there were sharks, whales, octopuses, and other demon beasts baring their sharp teeth and fixing their eyes on him like he was their prey.

Upon hearing that Lu Yang wanted to see him, Dai Bufan emerged from the ball of water, his body returning to its original size. He opened his mouth and swallowed the water sphere along with the ferocious demon beasts into his stomach.

This was one of his combat methods—dragging enemies into a water sphere and letting the demon beasts inside rip them apart.

“Let them in.”

Dai Bufan mused, Aside from Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, there’s also Li Haoran. Could the situation this time be related to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?

“Why is it that every time these two go on a mission, they get involved with a diabolic creed?” Dai Bufan was perplexed, suspecting that birds of the same feather flocked together, which was why the two and diabolic creeds were drawn to each other.

No matter what Lu Yang reports this time, nothing can surprise me anymore. I mean, what else could it be? At worst, it’ll be them successfully joining the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

When the three of them found Dai Bufan, Lu Yang honestly reported, “Senior Brother Dai, the three of us have established a new diabolic creed.”

Chapter 311: Yun Heavenly Sovereign and Dou Heavenly Sovereign

In that moment, Dai Bufan wished he could subdue the abomination that was Lu Yang, just like how the abbot of the Hanging Monastery had subdued the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

So you didn’t go to the Everlasting Creed to be a spy but for further training?

“Wait wait wait! It’s not what you think, Senior Brother Dai!” Seeing Dai Bufan on the verge of flipping out, Lu Yang quickly yelled that there was a misunderstanding.

Dai Bufan was at the Fusion Stage; even the Unbeatable Golden Core advised Lu Yang to commit suicide swiftly to maintain his win rate.

Lu Yang automatically blocked off the Unbeatable Golden Core’s suggestion.

“Tell me then, what’s going on?” Dai Bufan demanded an honest explanation from the three of them.

“Here's the thing. In Guhuai Town, we encountered three female ghosts who had soul restrictions placed on them by the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. To gain the trust of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, we claimed to be geniuses from the Heavenly Court in the ancient era and said that we had found Qin Haoran’s reincarnation...”

Dai Bufan, “...”

You two really know how to spin tales.

If I didn’t know Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s true nature, I would have believed that a Heavenly Court existed in the ancient era and that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were ancient geniuses who had recently revived with the goal of rebuilding it.

He had instinctively excluded Li Haoran. Based on my understanding of Li Haoran, he was probably just an actor playing his role in this.

Since even I am nearly convinced, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed would definitely buy it. Although the Nine-Netherworlds Creed mistaking Qin Yanyan as Qin Haoran’s reincarnation was unexpected, it doesn’t affect the overall plan.

“So, what do you need me to do?”

“Here’s the thing. Our Heavenly Court Creed currently has few members—just the four of us. We’re lacking someone who can intimidate the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. I was hoping you could help us find another follower for the Heavenly Court Creed, Senior Brother Dai.”

“Hey, Lu Yang, as the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign, am I not enough to intimidate a mere Nine-Netherworlds Creed?” Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wore an expression that said, “I’m super powerful.”

When Lu Yang was fabricating the Heavenly Court Creed, he had consulted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy multiple times. Not only did she provide multiple constructive ideas and assist Lu Yang in polishing the history and doctrines of the Heavenly Court Creed, but she also strongly recommended that Lu Yang place her in the highest position.

And thus, Lu Yang changed the original Yun Heavenly Sovereign to Dou Heavenly Sovereign.

Hope Big Senior Sister won’t mind.

Facing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang said solemnly, “Immortal Fairy, as the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign, how can you make a move so easily? It would tarnish your prestige.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy found his point valid and stopped throwing a tantrum.

Dai Bufan contemplated. Lu Yang’s nominal shifu is still in prison and can’t get away, while his actual shifu is someone I don’t dare to command. Meng Jingzhou’s shifu, Third Elder, has sufficient cultivation but not brains, which doesn’t make him an appropriate choice to participate in this.

“You can get Fifth Elder to help you.” Fifth Elder is staid in character, has sufficient cultivation, and is Li Haoran’s shifu. He’s the most suitable for this task.

~~~

After the three left, Dai Bufan called over the senior male disciple manning the front desk. “Regarding the three female ghosts mentioned in Lu Yang’s mission report, if there are no issues after investigation, bring them directly to the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Dai Bufan was worried that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed might secretly monitor the three female ghosts. If they sent someone to sound out the ghosts and the matter of the ghosts being registered with the Dao-Seeking Sect got exposed, it would be disastrous.

“Lu Yang and the others are still too young.”

~~~

“What? You are Junior Brother Li’s ex-daughter?” Hearing Qin Yanyan explain her identity, Tao Yaoye and Man Gu felt they had broadened their horizons.

Let’s first put aside the matter that Junior Brother Li was the previous creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. He’s so young, yet he already has a daughter older than himself?

Even within the Dao-Seeking Sect, this is quite absurd.

“Quick, tell us! What do you call Junior Brother Li? And after leaving his hometown, how did you end up at the Dao-Seeking Sect?” Tao Yaoye couldn’t hide her eagerness for gossip.

Qin Yanyan was somewhat overwhelmed by Tao Yaoye’s fervent questions, but fortunately, Lu Yang’s voice interrupted her.

“Junior Sister Tao, Junior Brother Man, have you formed your golden cores?” Lu Yang was quite surprised when he saw Tao Yaoye and Man Gu. They’re pretty fast in forming their golden cores.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou subconsciously glanced at Li Haoran. You’re the only one who hasn’t formed a golden core yet.

“Shoo shoo shoo! This is called ‘accumulating steadily and unleashing quickly!’ Slow and steady wins the race!” Li Haoran replied with a stormy expression.

Tao Yaoye revealed a sly smile. “It’s all thanks to Senior Brother Lu and Senior Brother Meng. Your experiences in forming your golden cores provided Junior Brother Man and me great inspiration.”

“What golden cores did you form?”

Just as Man Gu was about to answer, Tao Yaoye reached out her hand to stop him. Senior Brother Lu, it’s been a long time since we last sparred. Instead of asking us directly what kind of golden cores we formed, why don’t we see if you can guess on the arena stage?”

“Sure,” Lu Yang agreed with a smile. He hadn’t engaged in battle since forming his golden core.

“Then I’ll fight you, Junior Brother Man will fight Senior Brother Meng, while Junior Brother Li will watch.” Tao Yaoye had already decided who would be up against whom.

Meng Jingzhou was excited. After constantly fighting those above my level, it’s finally time to fight a genius at the same level. “Then let’s get on the arena stage?”

“Let’s go!”

They split into pairs and jumped onto a stage respectively.

Their actions attracted the interest of many disciples in the Dao-Seeking Sect, especially those in the same cohort as Lu Yang. The four of them on the stage were practically their idols.

“Who do you think will win?” Qin Yanyan asked her ex-dad curiously.

Li Haoran rolled his eyes. “Who knows? In any case, I’m not qualified to participate.” But that shouldn’t be the case though. As the reincarnation of a formidable expert, I should have become the number one prodigy of the younger generation.

Upon closer thought, that scoundrel Qin Haoran had only left me a pair of mother and daughter unrelated to me by blood and past-life memories I would rather forget.

Qin Haoran, why are all your memories about solving the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s deficit crisis? Is there not a single one about fortuitous opportunities?!

“Rather than asking who will win, why not see for yourself?” An indifferent voice came from behind Qin Yanyan.

Turning her head, Qin Yanyan saw a cold and aloof woman standing behind her. The woman was a peerless beauty, like a snowy mountain that was hard to approach. Her black hair cascaded like a waterfall down to her waist, and she donned an elegant and celestial-like dress. Her demeanor was tranquil and calm, like an immortal fairy in the sky.

Qin Yanyan used to think that her mother was the most beautiful woman in the world, but she hadn’t expected there to be someone even more stunning than her mother.

“Jiejie, who are you?”

Hearing Yun Zhi’s voice, Li Haoran involuntarily broke out in a cold sweat. He quickly turned his head and saw that eternally expressionless face. Although he hadn’t done anything wrong, he couldn’t help but feel nervous in the presence of Yun Zhi. “Big...Big Senior Sister, you’re back.”

“Mmm, I just finished with my business and returned,” Yun Zhi replied, leaving Li Haoran unsure how to continue the conversation.

He thought, Forget it, I shall not think about it. Let’s just watch the fight.

Yun Zhi had brought back the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s kitchen and was about to look for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy when she heard that Lu Yang and the other three were sparring here.

I might as well check it out.

Chapter 312: Tao Yaoye’s Golden Core

At the Martial Plaza, Lu Yang stood with his hands behind his back, the red tassel on the hilt of his sword swaying in the wind. The corners of his mouth were tugged into a faint smile, as if the outcome of the battle was within his grasp.

In stark contrast, Tao Yaoye looked like she was facing a formidable enemy. Her golden core had given her the confidence to challenge Lu Yang, but that confidence was all she had. Deep down, she was uncertain whether her golden core could triumph over Lu Yang.

“Unbeatable Golden Core, how can I defeat Tao Yaoye?” Lu Yang felt it was necessary to let Tao Yaoye understand the power of his golden core.

The Unbeatable Golden Core quickly produced a concise yet effective answer. “Use the Arhat Fist.”

Lu Yang suddenly remembered that he was capable of this unique art. The Lu-Style Arhat Fist—one punch, one bald. It’s particularly effective against women.

When Tao Yaoye saw Lu Yang reveal a self-assured smile as if he had thought of something, her face immediately turned pallid.

“Senior Brother Lu, we’re fellow disciples. Please, whatever you do, don’t use the Arhat Fist!”

“...Fine.” Lu Yang pondered for a bit and agreed. After all, we are fellow disciples. There’s no need to take things so far.

“Arhat Fist? Is that the Buddhist art that allows one to transform into an arhat upon major success in mastery?” The disciples below the stage whispered among themselves, not understanding why Tao Yaoye was so scared of the Arhat Fist.

“It should be. As far as I know, there’s no other Arhat Fist in the world.”

“Although the Arhat Fist is incredibly powerful, with Junior Sister Tao’s talent, she shouldn’t be this afraid of it, right?”

“Not sure.”

No matter how knowledgeable and experienced these disciples were, they still didn’t know the inside story.

Qin Yanyan was equally puzzled and asked Yun Zhi. “Jiejie, do you know why?” Li Haoran and I are past-life father and daughter, and my mother hasn’t married him yet, so we are considered the same generation. Since Yun Zhi is Li Haoran’s senior sister, there should be no problem with me calling her “jiejie.”

She wasn’t sure if it was just a figment of her imagination, but she couldn’t help but see an almost imperceptible smile on Yun Zhi’s visage. “Compared to the ordinary Arhat Fist, Lu Yang’s version causes people to lose their hair.”

“What?” Qin Yanyan was stunned, thinking she had misheard. I’ve never heard of such a fist technique before.

Is this the talent of the number one person of the younger generation?

On the stage, Lu Yang held his sword, its light flickering like flowing stars.

Tao Yaoye opened her red paper umbrella, spinning it gently and creating ripples in space.

Lu Yang was shocked to discover that the audience around him had disappeared, and the arena beneath his feet expanded endlessly, with no boundaries in sight.

His heart tightened as he realized he had fallen into Tao Yaoye’s illusory domain. If he thought the stage was truly boundless and fought carelessly, he might accidentally fall off the stage and lose the match.

Lu Yang raised his sword toward Tao Yaoye while simultaneously activating the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra to break the illusion.

The red paper umbrella closed and shielded Tao Yaoye. She could feel the force transmitted through Lu Yang’s sword and knew she couldn’t fight him head-on. With an elegant gait, she retreated backward.

But how could Lu Yang let this opportunity slip? He pursued her relentlessly. However, the red paper umbrella seemed to be made of some unknown material that could surprisingly block the continuous attacks from the Qingfeng Sword.

Tao Yaoye tried every trick to outmaneuver Lu Yang, hoping to make him accidentally step off the stage. Yet, no matter what she tried, Lu Yang lingered at the edge of the stage, simply never taking a step beyond it.

“You saw through my illusion again!” Tao Yaoye exclaimed bitterly. She was confident in her illusions. Even when Golden Core cultivators knew they were trapped in her illusion, they couldn’t see through it. Only Lu Yang could instantly break it.

“Not bad, Junior Sister Tao. In the past, my cultivation technique would automatically activate to break your illusions. This time, I had to activate it myself.”

While complimenting her, Lu Yang’s sword moves became even fiercer. Even if the red paper umbrella was made of a special material, Tao Yaoye’s body couldn’t withstand the strain of such high-intensity combat. Every time they clashed, the impact would leave her arms numb.

“Slash!” Sword light dwindled and then exploded in an instant, forming an arc in the air. Unable to resist, Tao Yaoye was sent flying.

She took advantage of this opportunity to distance herself from Lu Yang. She opened her red umbrella, and with a flick, another Tao Yaoye was created.

Now, there were two Tao Yaoyes on stage, both holding red umbrellas and smiling sweetly, making it hard to distinguish them.

“Senior Brother Lu, didn’t you want to know what kind of golden core I formed? Then please don’t use your cultivation technique.” Tao Yaoye felt helpless. Her illusions should have given her an advantage against anyone, but Lu Yang’s technique was born to counter hers. My high-level illusions are all like child’s play in front of him.

“I won’t use it then!” Lu Yang was true to his word. He took out the Twin Lotus Flower seeds and used the Tree-Planting Mantra. The lotus bloomed, and two Lu Yangs appeared.

The audience erupted in murmurs. These disciples had never seen such a Clone Technique before.

Lu Yang’s junior brothers and sisters looked at him with admiration sparkling in their eyes. As expected of Senior Brother Lu! Even his techniques are different from normal people.

The two Lu Yangs attacked the Tao Yaoyes at the same time.

One of these two Tao Yaoyes has to be an Illusory Clone. Illusory Clones could use spells and techniques but couldn’t physically collide, so Lu Yang should be able to identify which was real and which was fake upon contact.

Bang!

Bang!

The sound of two collisions reverberated through the air. Lu Yang was slightly stunned. Both Tao Yaoyes could engage in close combat. Could Junior Sister Tao have learned a real Clone Technique?

No, Junior Sister Tao must be using illusions. Otherwise, she wouldn’t have asked me not to use my technique. But if she’s using illusions, how do I explain why both Tao Yaoyes felt real?

Yun Zhi, who had been watching the battle, nodded slightly. She found Tao Yaoye’s golden core truly interesting. It’s also an unprecedented type of golden core.

“One of them must be fake!” Lu Yang made his judgment. As his sword danced, its rays gleamed like a dragon, thrusting toward one of the Tao Yaoyes.

Lu Yang’s clone also attacked the other Tao Yaoye.

“Break!” Lu Yang hollered as he unleashed the Breaking Word Mantra.

Both Tao Yaoyes felt a flash of white light before something cold came into contact with their necks—the Qingfeng Sword was resting on their necks.

Lu Yang frowned. Even at the end of the battle, he still couldn’t discern which Tao Yaoye was real. Thus, he had no choice but to use his absolute strength to defeat both Tao Yaoyes.

A bold guess began to form in Lu Yang’s mind.

“How’s that, Senior Brother Lu? Did you figure it out?” Tao Yaoye wasn’t upset about losing. With Lu Yang’s cultivation technique, I had no chance of winning anyway.

“A golden core with the ability to switch between reality and illusion?”

Tao Yaoye’s mouth opened slightly, not expecting Lu Yang to have deduced most of it.

“More or less. This is a completely new type of golden core. When I cast illusions, the biggest problem was people figuring out which is real and which is an illusion. But my golden core circumvents this problem.

“Take the earlier example. Both clones could be real, or both could be fake. The key lies in how the opponent perceives them. If you believe both are real, then they are real. If you believe both are fake, then they are fake.

“Senior Brother Lu, you kept hesitating, uncertain which was real and which was fake, so you were constantly testing it out. Since you couldn’t come to a resolution, both of them were the real me.

“The only way to break the illusion is to firmly believe that one is real and the other is fake, then focus your attack on the one you believe is the real me.

“And that is my golden core—the Illusion-Reality At Will Golden Core.”

“Little Junior Brother.”

Lu Yang looked up and realized Yun Zhi had also been watching the battle. He jumped off the stage and stood obediently in front of her, wearing a flattering smile. “Big Senior Sister, you’re back.”

Qin Yanyan was startled. This was her first time seeing Lu Yang so well-behaved.

Chapter 313: Meng Jingzhou Achieves Enlightenment on the Arena Stage

“Not bad at all. I thought that your swordsmanship fundamentals might not keep up with your current cultivation after advancing to the Golden Core Stage. I was going to remind you, but it seems that my concerns were unnecessary.”

“It’s all because you taught well, Big Senior Sister.”

How could Lu Yang dare to slack off in training his fundamentals? He recalled the early days of his cultivation. Big Senior Sister had me play with tofu during the day and soak in boiling water baths at night to hone my fundamentals. If not for the ample supply of miracle medicine, it’s hard to say whether I’d have made it out alive. Should Big Senior Sister discover that my fundamentals are not solid and subject me to all that again... Lu Yang shuddered at the thought.

I absolutely can’t go through all that again!

“Little Tao, it’s good that you have comprehended a yin-yang transformation golden core from the Twin Lotus Flower and linked it to illusion techniques. But don’t forget that you also possess the Metamorphic Immortal Physique. Don’t neglect to develop it.”

“Yes, Big Senior Sister!”

“Alright, the two of you can review this battle later. For now, let’s watch Little Meng and Little Man’s fight.”

“These two have been fighting for so long?” Tao Yaoye was floored. She and Lu Yang had fought for quite some time, but she hadn’t expected Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu to last even longer.
