“Both of them are physique cultivators, so it’s not easy to determine a winner.” Lu Yang was not surprised. Meng Jingzhou’s golden core had wondrous effects against demons and monsters, but it was useless against Man Gu, who was also a physique cultivator.

Man Gu held a demon beast’s leg bone, a trophy he had obtained from the jungle after slaying a Nascent Soul demon beast with Tao Yaoye. Swinging the leg bone, he howled like a man in the wild, his eyes filled with madness and savagery.

Lu Yang was bewildered. He had never seen Man Gu in such a state before, and this behavior didn’t seem to align with Man Gu’s usual personality. Man Gu fought with brute strength, but he was never this frenzied, like he was hunting demon beasts in the wilderness.

Meng Jingzhou was also startled by Man Gu’s appearance and lost the initiative in the fight. Overwhelmed from the outset, he poured most of his effort into defense, rarely finding an opening to strike back.

Although Man Gu’s fighting style seemed wild, a closer inspection revealed a refined layer beneath the brute force. It was an approach that balanced offense and defense, the product of countless trials and constant refinement.

“Hmm? This fighting style looks familiar! It’s just like the barbarians I’ve encountered before. With stones and bones in hand, they’d charge forward, relentlessly pounding the enemies’ skulls until their brains spilled out.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was excited to recognize something familiar.

Lu Yang was baffled. “Is this the fighting style of the Ancient Barbarians? But why did I hear that their fighting style has been lost to time?” The Barbarian Tribe’s lineage had severe gaps of discontinuity, and records of the ancient era were scarce.

“You’ve forgotten? Man Gu’s bloodline was blessed by me. Just as demon beasts can pass down mighty abilities through their bloodlines, I can naturally do the same!”

When demon beasts reached a certain cultivation realm, the hidden legacy power in their bloodline would awaken, allowing them to master their innate mighty abilities. The Taotie[1] Tribe’s “Devour” and the Nine-Tailed Fox Tribe’s “Charm” were examples of this.

The purer the bloodline, the earlier the inherited powers awakened.

“By the way, what kind of golden core did Man Gu form?” Lu Yang turned to ask Tao Yaoye. There’s no need to keep it a secret now, right?

“Probably an unprecedented golden core too. I think it’s called Ancestor Assembly Golden Core. It allows him to summon the souls and spirits of his deceased ancestors to possess him and aid him in battle.”

“So powerful?!” Lu Yang was flabbergasted. “Doesn’t this mean that the souls of the Ancient Barbarians are still around?”

Yun Zhi slowly shook her head. “It’s not what you think. Only an immortal could possess the power to keep a soul from dissipating for three hundred thousand years.”

“Then what’s going on with Man Gu?”

“Although the souls of Man Gu’s ancestors had dissipated and returned to heaven and earth, they are still connected to him through their shared bloodline. His ancestors sensed the presence of the Barbarian Tribe and reassembled a portion of their vanished souls to descend into Man Gu’s body through the Ancient Barbarian bloodline. However, this possession method stems from one’s mindless instincts.”

Lu Yang was reminded of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. This is somewhat similar to her method, but far less incredible.

“So Meng Jingzhou’s opponent isn’t just Man Gu but an entire Ancient Barbarian Tribe?” Lu Yang felt that Meng Jingzhou was in for a tough fight.

The Ancient Barbarians were a race that followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Fighting was as common to them as eating, and they had plentiful combat experience. How could Meng Jingzhou be their match?

On the arena stage, the attacks pushed Meng Jingzhou back step by step. He couldn’t unleash his Arhat Fist or Heaven-Shaking Six Forms properly.

Man Gu’s eyes were vacant, completely taken over by his Ancient Barbarian ancestors. His fighting was driven by primal instinct alone.

In terms of physical strength, Meng Jingzhou held a slight edge over Man Gu, but he couldn’t compete with Man Gu’s wealth of experience. The combined combat experience of the Ancient Barbarian ancestors amounted to hundreds of thousands of years; Meng Jingzhou stood no chance against that. Although Man Gu had the upper hand and was suppressing Meng Jingzhou, he still couldn’t defeat him outright in a short time.

“Does Meng Jingzhou seem a bit off?”

Meng Jingzhou felt himself entering a strange state. Within his body, his two Single’s Golden Cores sensed Man Gu’s golden core and began to spin uncontrollably, as if provoked. They were like two miniature suns that radiated warmth through him. His body felt transparent and revitalized, and his acupoints opened, each one absorbing and expelling spirit qi.

As the two golden cores spun, Meng Jingzhou’s mind emptied, and his past experiences flooded his brain, with his old memories compressed to their limit. Then, with a deafening boom, they exploded in his mind.

Meng Jingzhou’s head swayed slightly, and he felt that the world seemed clearer than ever before.

“Did I just achieve enlightenment and comprehend a new fist technique?” Meng Jingzhou clenched his fist in disbelief.

He had heard that the state of enlightenment was rare and hard to come by. Most cultivators never experienced it in their lifetimes. Yet, here I am, already achieving enlightenment at the Golden Core Stage? Moreover, judging by what just happened, it seemed like my two Single’s Golden Cores had assisted me in my enlightenment?

“I knew my Single’s Golden Cores were unbeatable!”

As Meng Jingzhou mentally rehearsed the new fist technique, his expression turned peculiar. “This fist technique seems...”

“Wait, stop!” Meng Jingzhou reached out, stopping Man Gu from attacking. “I just comprehended a new fist technique. Barbarian ancestors, if you insist on fighting, don’t blame me for activating it!”

Man Gu froze in place, seemingly waiting to hear what else Meng Jingzhou had to say.

“The fist technique I have comprehended involves the power of karma, curses, as well as the accumulated resentment of my Single’s Lineage. Anyone struck by my fists will be cursed to remain single for life, just like me. This is a karmic curse!

“I shall name it the Single’s Curse Fist!

“This should be the inherent fist technique of my Double Single’s Golden Cores! If you are willing to let Man Gu take this punch, then by all means, keep attacking me!”

The Ancient Barbarian ancestors hurriedly made Man Gu’s body jump off the stage and concede defeat. Their instincts told them that Meng Jingzhou was telling the truth!

1. The taotie is a gluttonous beast in Chinese mythology. It is popular as a decorative element on Chinese artifacts, such as bronze vessels. ☜

Chapter 314: Fist Techniques and Spells Are Both Methods

“He mastered a curse-type fist technique, or should I say, a curse-type spell, all by himself?!” Even the knowledgeable senior male disciples in the crowd were taken aback.

The Dao of Curse fell under the domain of karma. Both karma and time were universally acknowledged in the cultivation world as one of the mighty abilities that were the most difficult to comprehend, learn, and unravel.

Junior Brother Li is so young, yet he comprehended such a ruthless curse-type spell on his own. Who could have thought?

“To even ask whether this is a fist technique or a spell clearly shows you haven’t been paying attention during Big Senior Sister’s classes!” A Divine Transfiguration male disciple looked at his Nascent Soul junior sister disdainfully for shouting earlier. “With your lack of knowledge and skills, how do you expect to advance to the Divine Transfiguration Stage in the future?”

The Nascent Soul junior sister stammered. In the outside world, she was renowned for her brilliance and erudition, revered and praised as a “talented lady.” But within the Dao-Seeking Sect, such accolades were utterly meaningless.

Who would dare claim to be well-read and erudite in the Dao-Seeking Sect?

“Big Senior Sister has repeatedly emphasized not to draw too clear a line between fist techniques and spells. Fist techniques and spells are all methods.[1] All methods ultimately lead to the same destination. If you make such rigid distinctions, how will you ever achieve the state of ‘one method to connect all methods?’

“It’s precisely because many people like you have this misconception that despite possessing powerful spells far superior to their opponents, they end up defeated after their opponents seize the opportunity to engage in close combat.”

Cultivators proficient in spells feared close combat the most. Having spent years honing their spells, their physical strength was often mediocre. Once entangled in close combat, not only would they be unable to cast spells, but even their safety couldn’t be assured.

The Divine Transfiguration senior male disciple patiently explained, “So the ideal state is to use fist techniques to cast spells. That way, regardless of whether it’s long-range spell battles or close-quarters physical combat, there will be no weaknesses, right?”

The Nascent Soul junior female disciple nodded. It does make sense. Although I have ample energy and practice both fist techniques and spells without neglecting either, Senior Brother’s words have made me realize that I should reflect on myself.

“Big Senior Sister even complimented Junior Brother Lu Yang, saying he has achieved this, demonstrating signs of unifying all methods to lead to the same destination. He’s far ahead of you and me.

“Although I don’t know to what extent Junior Brother Li has accomplished, if he could earn Big Senior Sister’s praise, he must have made remarkable progress in this aspect!”

Although the senior disciples had lined up to beat Lu Yang up, that didn’t stop them from acknowledging his talent.

~~~

Lu Yang, Tao Yaoye, and the others were astonished to see Meng Jingzhou achieve enlightenment and comprehend the “Descendants-Severing Fist Technique.”

How could such a fist technique exist? Is there no more justice in the world?

The person most shocked was Qin Yanyan.

Before coming to the Dao-Seeking Sect, she carried some pride, thinking that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were simply faster in their cultivation. She believed that she could catch up with some effort.

Although she was two months older than Li Haoran, her cultivation was on par with his. Since Li Haoran’s talent ranked among the top ten of the younger generation, she figured she wasn’t far behind and was fully qualified to become a disciple of one of the Five Great Immortal Sects. However, with Su Yiren as her mentor, there was no need for her to join one of the sects.

She had believed that even if there was a gap between her and young top talents like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, it wasn’t significant. By observing their battles, she could surely learn something.

But now? The day anyone manages to learn it is when pigs fly!

No wonder my ex-dad can only rank fifth in his cohort despite having the purest Fire Spirit Root. It’s indeed hard to break into the top four.

Moreover, the first place uses the Arhat Fist to make people lose their hair, while the second place uses the Single’s Curse Fist to make people single for life. Are these two from the Dao-Seeking Sect or the Hanging Monastery?

Upon witnessing Meng Jingzhou’s fist techniques, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy lamented, “So this is what they mean by ‘Talents rise in every generation, dominating the scene for centuries.’”[2]

Lu Yang raised an eyebrow, looking conflicted. The poem was recited correctly, but why can’t I help but feel that it’s somewhat out of place in this context?

“Does this kind of fist technique have no limitations?” Tao Yaoye wondered. Man Gu’s Ancestor Assembly Golden Core was within reasonable bounds, not to the point of synchronizing with the cultivation levels of his ancestors. Could Meng Jingzhou’s fist technique really ignore cultivation levels?

Wouldn’t everyone run at the sight of it then?

Yun Zhi watched the smug Meng Jingzhou for a while before withdrawing her gaze. She shook her head lightly and explained to everyone. “It’s not as exaggerated as you think. Meng Jingzhou is at the Golden Core Stage, so his fist technique can only be used against cultivators at the Golden Core Stage or below. Furthermore, he has to be wary of backlash from his opponents.”

“Backlash?”

“Yes, take Li Haoran as an example. His fiancée is Su Yiren, a Fusion cultivator. Li Haoran’s destined match is Su Yiren, and such a marital fate cannot be severed by ordinary means. If Meng Jingzhou were to use the Single’s Curse Fist on Li Haoran, he would suffer a backlash from being unable to overcome Li Haoran’s marital fate.”

Lu Yang asked curiously, “What would happen to Meng Jingzhou if he suffers a backlash?” Would it mean that Meng Jingzhou himself will be doomed to singlehood?

But in that case, wouldn’t there be no difference regardless of whether he suffers a backlash?

Yun Zhi performed a quick divination with her fingers. “He might lose all karmic ties with women for a period of time. Specifically, during this period, he’d be unable to interact with any women. By the workings of fate and coincidences, he might find himself avoiding women or women avoiding him.”

The Single’s Curse Fist sounds very restrictive, with the risk of backlash. But upon closer thought, who else would be like Li Haoran and have a Fusion fiancée at such a young age?

Li Haoran, who was also listening nearby, was baffled. “Isn’t the greatest backlash from Senior Brother Meng’s fist technique getting hunted down after using it?”

Lu Yang, “...”

That’s valid. Meng Jingzhou’s fist technique can’t kill anyone, but for anyone struck by it, swearing eternal vengeance against him would likely be the best-case scenario.

“Earlier, Senior Brother Meng mentioned that his fist technique is inherent to his golden core. But I’ve never heard of a Single’s Golden Core having such a technique?” Li Haoran wondered out loud. In his quest to form his golden core, he had read many insights on golden core formation, including descriptions of the Single’s Golden Core.

Li Haoran pointed out the flaw in Li Haoran’s thinking. “You got something wrong. Meng Jingzhou didn’t form just one Single’s Golden Core but an unprecedented two.”

Question marks were popping out of Li Haoran’s head.

Lu Yang continued, “Previous seniors with a Single’s Spirit Root didn’t comprehend this fist technique, which implies that their level of singleness wasn’t as profound as Meng Jingzhou’s.”

“Lu Yang, you’re slandering me again! This is clearly a testament to my exceptional comprehension!” Meng Jingzhou jumped off the stage, glaring at Lu Yang in rage.

Lu Yang shrugged, pretending he hadn’t said anything.

Man Gu slowly woke up and looked around in confusion at the noisy surroundings. “I lost?” After summoning his ancestors to possess him, he had no memory of everything that transpired.

Lu Yang said earnestly, “Your ancestors were worried about cutting off the clan’s lineage and admitted defeat.”

“Ah?” Man Gu blinked in befuddlement. Did Senior Brother Meng resort to underhanded tricks like “Monkey Steals the Peach,” attacking the opponent with one hand and grabbing their crotch with the other?[3]

He couldn’t have gone so far, right?

“Lu Yang, come back with me,” Yun Zhi said curtly before heading straight back to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

The disciples who had been watching the battle dispersed. Some returned to cultivate, some went to the scripture library, while others went on dates with their junior sisters.

Lu Yang had to jog to keep up with Yun Zhi’s pace.

“Big Senior Sister, has the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s kitchen been brought back?”

“Mmm.”

Inside his mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes lit up.

1. Unfortunately, I had to tweak it in the English version. In the original Chinese text, fist techniques are “quan fa,” while spells are “fa shu.” As you can see, both have the character “fa” in them. It can mean law or method, among other meanings. ☜

2. This poem is typically used to describe the literary scene and aims to challenge poets like Li Bai and Du Fu of the Tang Dynasty. It was written by Zhao Yi, a historian and poet in the mid-Qing Dynasty. ☜

3. To be more precise, the peach refers to the testicles... ☜

Chapter 315: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Scheme Against the Four Ancient Immortals Spanned the Ages

Heaven’s Gate Peak had a total of six structures.

The dust-covered cave abode of the Taciturn Daoist, which no one was willing to clean.

Yun Zhi’s humble dwelling.

Lu Yang’s cave abode.

The kitchen, where Lu Yang and Yun Zhi had their meals.

The Discussion Hall.

And the cave abode where the sect leader handled the affairs of the Dao-Seeking Sect, now requisitioned by Yun Zhi.

“Big Senior Sister, where is the Immortal Fairy’s kitchen?” Lu Yang looked left and right but didn’t see anything resembling a kitchen behind her.

“Don’t be impatient.” Yun Zhi rummaged in her sleeve for a while, then produced an exquisitely crafted architectural model about the size of her palm. It was a piece of jade with obvious signs of human craftsmanship.

“This is my kitchen!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy dashed out of the mental space in excitement.

“This is the Immortal Fairy’s kitchen? Why do I remember her kitchen being inside the Everlasting Immortal statue?” Lu Yang had thought that Yun Zhi would bring the whole statue over.

This time, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy took it upon herself to explain. “How could my kitchen have been inside the statue from the start? Clearly, someone used spatial abilities to embed my kitchen inside the statue. Little Lass Yun must have also used spatial abilities to move my kitchen out!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was getting too pleased with herself, referring to Yun Zhi as “Little Lass Yun” this time.

Yun Zhi didn’t mind such details and proceeded to consult the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “Senior, Heaven’s Gate Peak only has the two of us eating here. There’s no need for two kitchens. I plan to dismantle the existing kitchen and replace it with yours. How does that sound?”

Exclamation marks were shooting out of Lu Yang’s head.

“Sure,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy readily agreed. After all, a kitchen is meant to be used, and my kitchen is definitely far superior to the original one.

Yun Zhi extended her left hand to cast a seal at the original kitchen. After it automatically shrank, she stowed it away in her sleeve.

“Oh, this is Sleeve Cosmos!” There were many methods to shrink objects, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t sure which one it was earlier. But now that she had witnessed the casting process, she naturally identified Yun Zhi’s technique.

Sleeve Cosmos was a spatial method worthy enough to be called a mighty ability. Unlike storage rings, it could store not only inanimate items but also living beings, essentially creating a small world within the sleeve. It was often viewed as a symbol of an expert.

After all, to perform Sleeve Cosmos, one first needed to wear robes with wide sleeves. However, wearing wide-sleeved garments was highly disadvantageous in combat, so only those with absolute confidence would wear them.

Like Yun Zhi.

Like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“In the past, I often used this move too. I’d keep snacks in my sleeves and fish them out to eat whenever I had nothing to do.

“The sleeve can even accommodate a bed, so you can sleep wherever you want. Once, I passed by the sea and saw kun fish and jiao dragons swimming without restraint. I hurled my bed onto the seabed and lay down on the bed, enjoying the sea breeze as I drifted with the currents. It was incredibly comfortable!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy relished the memory, wishing it had lasted longer.

“This mighty ability is also a great choice for giving surprises.

“Weren’t Qilin Immortal and the rest too embarrassed to eat my cooking, always standing me up? Thus, I packed the meals I’d made into my sleeves and went to look for them. They thought it was just a regular visit and welcomed me. Once I entered their cave abodes, I suddenly pulled out the meals and gave them a surprise!”

Lu Yang tried to envision the scene for a second and felt his imagination was lacking. I can’t quite picture the level of despair in that.

“But this tactic can’t be used too often.”

“Why not?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scrunched up her nose. “It easily makes you smell like food.”

Yun Zhi tossed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s kitchen into the air, and it grew with the wind, becoming larger and larger until it was the same size as Lu Yang’s cave abode.

This wasn’t the kitchen’s largest state yet. The kitchen itself had been compressed by spatial spells, and its interior was impressively large. The last time Lu Yang and the others had seen it, they had taken just a glance; there were still many areas Lu Yang had yet to explore.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s right hand moved swiftly, looking like she was forming seals. “I’m granting you two access to my kitchen. From now on, the two of you can enter whenever you want. We’re all family, so don’t be shy.” Right as the words left her mouth, she flicked a seal toward Lu Yang.

It was a simple drawing of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy grinning foolishly.

Before Lu Yang could react, the seal entered his body and disappeared. He vaguely sensed a connection to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s kitchen, as if he could enter it with a single thought.

Yun Zhi didn’t stop him, allowing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s seal to enter her body as well.

“Speaking of which, I also gave this seal to the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other three immortals, allowing them to enter my kitchen as they wished. After my cave abode was built, I invited the four of them to visit. No matter what I said, they insisted on coming over only to take a look and that there was no need for me to cook for them.

“Being the beautiful and kind-hearted person I was, I felt bad. They had traveled all the way across several planets and light years. Since they were already here, why not have a meal before leaving?

“They were adamant about not eating, so I took a step back and said I’d give them the kitchen’s seal so that they could enter my kitchen at will.

“And they accepted it.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others were pretty curious. Whenever they got something new, they’d want to try it out. Hence, they used the seal to open the kitchen door and entered.”

“What happened after that?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flashed a mischievous grin. “I only said the seal allowed them to enter the kitchen freely. I didn’t say it allowed them to exit freely.” She harrumphed. “You think you can leave after entering the kitchen? They all must obediently stay put and eat.

“You know my cooking skills—they’re so good people wish they could lick the plates clean. After eating their fill, the four of them slept in the kitchen. Good thing I had placed a bed in there; otherwise, they would’ve had to sleep on the floor.

“After waking up, they bid goodbye and left my cave abode.”

Lu Yang felt a shiver run through him, and a scene began to play in his mind.

On a dark and windy night, four young men seized the chance to explore an abandoned castle. They slowly pushed open the castle gates, only to find it pitch black inside. Even the moonlight was swallowed by the castle.

Suddenly, the castle gates slammed shut with a deafening bang, and lamps fueled by human oil lit up one by one. The mistress of the castle descended from above, an eerie smile stretched across her face as she cackled. “Now that you’re here, don’t dream of leaving.”

The four young men trembled in fear, regretting their decision to explore the castle.

If this tale were passed down to later generations, it might be recounted like this: the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s scheme spanned the ages, single-handedly outwitting the four ancient immortals and securing a great victory, while the four ancient immortals remained unconscious.

Such terrifying wisdom.

Lu Yang suddenly registered what had transpired. “Wait, the seal you just gave us...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy said nonchalantly, “Aiya, after they finished one meal, I gave them the seal that allows free entry and exit. It’s the same for you two.”

Chapter 316: Lu Yang Is Gone

Lu Yang deeply regretted entertaining the thought of entering the kitchen.

After obtaining the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s seal, he sensed a connection with the kitchen, as if a single thought could transport him inside.

Then, with a single thought, he was truly transported inside.

Lu Yang turned on his heel, throwing himself against the door in a desperate attempt to escape. Unfortunately for him, he was a mere mortal with a low cultivation realm. His efforts to push open the door were as futile as a mayfly trying to shake a giant tree—utterly useless. Even when he mustered every ounce of strength, the door didn’t

Putting aside the fact that he was a mortal, he reckoned that even an immortal wouldn’t help. Otherwise, why didn’t those four immortals leave back then? And after they woke up, why did they drag the Nine-Layers Immortal, who had encouraged the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to cook, outside to beat him up secretly?

There were reasons for all of that.

“Little Junior Brother, why are you running?” Yun Zhi was bewildered.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was the only one among the five ancient immortals who knew how to cook, which made her a unique spirit chef in the world. Why not cherish the opportunity to eat her cooking?

Besides, with the gaps in the passing down of ancient legacies, no one knows how cultivators cooked in the ancient era. Only a living fossil like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy can recreate the ancient culinary arts.

Previously, when the Five-Elements Sect visited, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had painstakingly prepared a feast. But before Yun Zhi could taste it, the furious sect leader of the Five-Elements Sect had flipped the table.

As for things like adding salt for twenty seconds, that was probably just a cooking habit from the ancient era.

Those dangerous immortal treasures or kitchen tools from the Everlasting Creed were also likely refined by the creed after acquiring them. The original tools were probably not so hazardous.

Besides, this is a rare learning opportunity. We should cherish it.

A spirit chef was highly welcomed no matter where they went. Yun Zhi believed that if Lu Yang could learn even a fraction of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s skills, he would be able to roam the Central Continent freely.

Just as Lu Yang was about to explain, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy interrupted him. “Exactly, why are you running? It’s rare that I’m willing to cook for you. This is a privilege reserved for immortals.” She furrowed her eyebrows, dissatisfied with Lu Yang’s reaction.

Then, she looked like she realized something. “Oh, I get it! You think my status is too high and that it’s beneath me to cook for you, so you feel guilty eating my food, right?

“Aiya, it’s fine. I’m not that particular. You’ve followed me for so long; don’t you know what kind of person I am?

“Come, let me borrow your body. I’ll return it to you after I’m done cooking. You’ll get to eat your meal later!” Since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t interact with physical objects, she needed to borrow Lu Yang’s body temporarily.

“Little Junior Brother, let Senior use it then.” Yun Zhi found the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s request perfectly reasonable.

Lu Yang wanted to resist, but was caught off guard by Yun Zhi’s words. In that moment of daze, his body was seized by the overjoyed Everlasting Immortal Fairy. He could only watch helplessly as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy took control of his body.

“This body isn’t strong enough. It can’t even withstand an explosion; it won’t be able to handle premium dishes,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy commented with a hint of disdain.

Lu Yang’s body was undoubtedly one of the strongest among Golden Core cultivators, but it was still a far cry from what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy required.

“Hold on, why would cooking involve explosions?” Lu Yang asked warily.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy found Lu Yang’s reaction strange. “Isn’t it normal? Don’t they all say that the finest delicacies explode on your taste buds the moment they enter your mouth?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Yun Zhi nodded subtly, taking mental notes of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words. These must be insights based on Senior Immortal Fairy’s experience. As a junior, I should be humble in learning.

“This time, make sure to study hard. I can groom you as my successor!” The first-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage said to the second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage.

The second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage was naturally both honored and terrified.

“Your body can’t handle dishes that are too challenging. Let me think... oh, I know! Let’s make Tomato and Egg Stir-Fry!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy came to a decision quickly.

Lu Yang breathed a small sigh of relief. You should have said so earlier. I know how to make this dish. It’s very simple; there’s no way the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would mess it up.

“What’s in this jar again?” As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy opened a medicine jar, a pungent smell wafted out.

Inside the mental space, Lu Yang felt like the world was spinning around him and swayed a couple of times. Before passing out, he mumbled, “What’s in the jar...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was fully focused on cooking and didn’t notice something unusual with Lu Yang. Now that she had control of Lu Yang’s body, his consciousness, or lack thereof, didn’t matter.

“Look, you need to stir vigorously when beating eggs, like this,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained the cooking steps while Yun Zhi listened attentively by her side.

“The egg mixture is for the Tomato and Egg Stir-Fry, and the leftover eggshells can be used to make soup. As the saying goes, ‘use the original soup base to digest the original hard-to-digest food’[1] This is what it means.”

Yun Zhi nodded from time to time, feeling that cooking methods in the ancient era were truly different from the modern era. There’s still much to learn.

Her current cultivation was not solely the result of her talent in comprehension but also her diligence and inquisitive nature. However, seldom were there things she needed to learn nowadays.

~~~

When Lu Yang groggily woke up, he found himself seated at the dining table, with dishes prepared by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy laid out before him. Across from him sat Yun Zhi, poised and elegant.

“You’re awake? You were busy managing the overall situation in Guhuai Town. Even after returning, you had to spar with Tao Yaoye and didn’t get to rest. You must have been too tired and fell asleep,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained kindly, worried that Lu Yang might not understand what had happened.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy did have the talent to show in cooking. The Tomato and Egg Stir-Fry was a vibrant mix of red and yellow, their colors appetizing and dazzling. The tantalizing aroma was enough to make anyone’s mouth water. Though it was a simple home-cooked dish, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had elevated it into something spectacular.

As for the eggshell soup placed at the side, Lu Yang automatically ignored it.

His appetite was whetted. Picking up a piece of tomato, he put it in his mouth.

“How is it? Does the egg taste good?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang expectantly.

“Hmm, egg?” Lu Yang remembered picking up something red.

“That’s right. I added some chili powder to the eggs.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, how much chili powder did you add to make the eggs as red as tomatoes?!

His vision went dark as he passed out from the spice.

“Why did he fall asleep again... oh no, is he allergic to chili?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was visibly concerned.

Yun Zhi remembered that Lu Yang could handle spicy food and analyzed, “Perhaps the spirit energy encompassed in the food was so intense that he fainted. But that’s a good thing. It can help him gradually absorb the spirit energy in the food and consolidate his cultivation.”

The chili powder was good stuff the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had hidden; it was a true immortal-tier delicacy.

“I see. By the way, how is my cooking?”

Yun Zhi gently picked up a piece of egg and chewed it carefully. The spiciness burst forth, and the spirit energy contained in the chili powder gushed toward her taste buds, leaving an unforgettable aftertaste.

“Absolutely delicious.”

“That’s great then. I was worried my culinary skills had lost their touch.”

1. The most direct translation would be “original soup digests original food,” but I modified it a little so that it’s hopefully easier to understand. It’s an eating habit where people drink the soup after eating the noodles or jiaozi. For some, it may just be a habit, while for others, they may find it nourishing or think it helps to digest the more starchy food. ☜

Chapter 317: Fifth Elder’s Whimsical Yet Ingenious Idea

“It’s a pity Lu Yang didn’t learn my Immortal Fairy Fist Technique. Otherwise, he wouldn’t have passed out.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that Lu Yang was great in every way, except for his stubborn refusal to learn her fist technique.

“Immortal Fairy Fist Technique?” Yun Zhi repeated softly. She put down her chopsticks, a trace of interest glinting in her eyes.

“It’s also called the Health Maintenance (Yangsheng) Fist Technique. Once mastered, your body becomes like medicine. You will no longer have to take pills when you’re sick or cultivating, and no poison in the world will affect you.

“However, to learn the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique, you must first master over a thousand other fist techniques, including the Arhat Fruit Fist, Malva Nut Fist,[1] and Ginseng Fist. You have to integrate them, discard what is false and retain what is true, sieve out the dregs and preserve the essence, and use your body as a furnace to merge these techniques into one body. That is the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique.”

Yun Zhi fell silent for a moment. Then, she stood up and asked solemnly, “Senior, could you teach me?”

“Of course.”

~~~

When Lu Yang woke up, he was no longer in the kitchen. fгeewebnovёl.com

“You’re awake? How do you feel?”

Lu Yang replied in his mind, I passed out from the spiciness, and you’re still asking me how I feel?

“My cultivation...” After stretching a little, Lu Yang noticed that his cultivation had actually improved slightly, advancing from the Basic Golden Core Stage to the Intermediate Golden Core Stage.

But I didn’t do anything.

“Hehe, did you think I just made an ordinary plate of Tomato and Egg Stir-Fry? No way! What I made was Tomato and Egg Stir-Fry that boosts your cultivation! You barely feel the improvement because you only took one bite. If you had finished the whole plate, I guarantee you’d have advanced to the Advanced Golden Core Stage!”

Lu Yang felt that although his step-by-step cultivation progress was slow, it was at least safe. If he followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s logic and ate the whole plate, he was afraid he might metamorphose and ascend to an immortal on the spot.

Outside the cave abode, Meng Jingzhou hollered, “Lu Yang, are you awake?”

“Yes, I’m awake.” As Lu Yang stepped out of the cave abode, he squinted under the blinding sunlight.

Standing at the entrance of the cave abode were Meng Jingzhou, Li Haoran, and Qin Yanyan.

Seeing that Lu Yang was awake, Meng Jingzhou heaved a sigh of relief. “You’re finally awake! You’ve been unconscious for three months!”

Lu Yang was floored. I didn’t expect the “medical potency” of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s poison to be so strong.

Li Haoran said helplessly, “Senior Brother Meng, Senior Brother Lu was only asleep for two hours.”

“Hey, Junior Brother Li, that’s not fair. It wasn’t easy for me to successfully trick Lu Yang once, yet you just had to expose me.”

Qin Yanyan silently observed this scene, wondering if the exceptional wit of the two peerless prodigies, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, was honed by integrating schemes and deceit into their daily lives.

It’s very likely.

“Come on, let’s go find Fifth Elder. If he joins the Heavenly Court Sect, he’ll be considered an elder-level member!”

~~~

With Li Haoran leading the way, the group soon found Fifth Elder, who was in the middle of refining artifacts.

Fifth Elder tossed his Daoist robe into the fire, subjecting it to the test of the raging flames. When the robe was scorched red, he reached in and pulled it out, his expression unchanged throughout the process.

He took a small hammer from his waist and began hitting the robe, producing a series of clanging sounds. Then, he plunged the robe into water, and a hiss marked the end of the refining process.

Fifth Elder looked at the newly refined Daoist robe in satisfaction and casually put it on. Only then did he realize that Lu Yang and the others were watching from nearby.

“Oh, it’s Little Lu.”

“Fifth Elder, are you refining clothes?” Lu Yang asked with uncertainty. The process looked less like refining clothes and more like forging some metal magical artifact.

“I’m trying to combine clothing and transportation tools.”

“Combine them?” Everyone was bewildered. Was there any connection between the two?

“How are they not related?” As a grandmaster of artifact refinement, Fifth Elder proceeded to explain. “Transportation tools, be it carriages or flying vessels, are all to make your travel more convenient, right?

“Carriages, flying vessels, and flying swords all have one thing in common—they can carry us. In that case, why have we always overlooked the most common thing that carries us—clothing?”

Lu Yang contemplated and realized it did make sense. From another perspective, when we wear clothes, aren’t they essentially wrapping around our bodies?

People are the carriers of clothing.

“Therefore, I believe that clothing is the most suitable mode of transportation. Watch this.” Fifth Elder activated his powers, and the refined Daoist robe floated upward, carrying him along with it.

After spinning once in the air, he landed smoothly and continued speaking. “Normally, only Golden Core cultivators can fly on their own, with the exception of sword cultivators, who can already fly on their sword at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

“If Foundation Establishment sword cultivators can fly on swords, why can’t ordinary Foundation Establishment cultivators fly with clothes?

“Of course, my current method of refining clothing is too complicated, and I still can’t make it accessible to Foundation Establishment cultivators. But once I’ve streamlined and simplified the process, registered a patent, and promoted it in the cultivation world, wouldn’t endless wealth flow into Artifact Refinement Peak?” Fifth Elder’s eyebrows seemed to dance with exultation as he spoke. Once the Artifact Refinement Peak has money, we can buy more materials and craft even better magical treasures.

“Fifth Elder, you’re a genius!” Lu Yang’s words were heartfelt. He believed the idea was highly feasible.

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s inexhaustible supply of spirit stones was thanks to geniuses like the Fifth Elder and Seventh Elder, who excelled in artifact refinement and pill concoction respectively. In particular, their artifact refining skills and achievements received widespread acclaim in the cultivation world.

“Who’s this little lass?” Fifth Elder pointed at Qin Yanyan.

“This is Junior Brother Li’s ex-wife’s daughter,” Lu Yang introduced.

Fifth Elder jumped in shock. When did my disciple get married?

“It’s my ex-life’s wife’s daughter!” Li Haoran quickly added.

Realization struck Fifth Elder. “Oh, Qin Yanyan, right? Haoran has mentioned you. That means you are my grand-disciple.”

Qin Yanyan, “...”

She was starting to regret coming to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Not only did she have the lowest seniority here with Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou constantly calling her “niece,” but now she had also become someone’s grand-disciple.

Qin Yanyan was just about to say that her past life and current life shouldn’t be conflated when she saw Fifth Elder fish out a magical treasure from the front of his robe.

“As this is our first meeting, it’s only proper that I give you a gift. I don’t have anything valuable on hand, but since you look like a talisman cultivator, do take this talisman-making brush. It’s inscribed with eighteen common talismans. With a bit of power, you can instantly draw them. It should be helpful to you.”

Qin Yanyan was startled by the magical artifact’s capabilities. A talisman-making brush was an essential tool for talisman cultivators, and she owned one herself. It was inscribed with ten talismans and crafted by a renowned veteran artifact-refining master at Su Yiren’s request. The master even said that a Golden Core talisman-making brush could only be engraved with up to ten types of talismans.

“This...this is too precious. I can’t accept it.”

“Just take it. It’s a little thing I made in my spare time, not worth much,” Fifth Elder said generously.

Li Haoran looked at Qin Yanyan with sourness pouring into his heart. Why did Shifu give Qin Yanyan a gift upon their first meeting, while his gift for our first meeting is throwing me into lava?

“By the way, why are you looking for me?” Fifth Elder finally recalled that Lu Yang and the others must have come for a reason.

“Basically, we have established the Heavenly Court Creed, which boasts a solid and ancient foundation, bolstered by ancient immortal legacies and support from prominent ancestral clans. One individual was once a half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, while another was the first successor of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

“Fifth Elder, we’d like to ask you to become a protector of our Heavenly Court Creed.”

Chapter 318: Deceiving the Nine-Netherworlds Creed Is a Tradition of the Dao-Seeking Sect

“The Heavenly Court Creed isn’t reputable, yet its foundation runs so deep?” Fifth Elder gasped. I’ve never heard of such a sect before.

Seeing that Fifth Elder was hoodwinked, Lu Yang continued, “In addition to the rich foundation, the Heavenly Court Creed will soon conduct another round of recruitment. There are already two candidates.

“One has an Innate Immortal Physique. The Nine-Layers Immortal, the first immortal in the ancient era, had managed to attain the Dao because of his Innate Immortal Physique.

“The other carries an entire race’s fortune and is blessed with immense luck. This individual is also both a Barbarian and a Confucian cultivator!

“Fifth Elder, what do you think? Do you want to join us?

“In our original plan, the Heavenly Court Creed will require a long time to grow, so that we can dominate the Battle of the Great Era. Unfortunately, the despicable Nine-Netherworlds Creed has set its sights on us. We need a protector to help us deal with them!”

Lu Yang cupped his fists and said solemnly, “Fifth Elder, if you are willing to lend a hand to the Heavenly Court Creed this time, we will surely repay you generously in the future!”

Fifth Elder fell silent for a moment. Just when Lu Yang thought Fifth Elder would agree, the latter slowly asked, “Have you registered the Heavenly Court Creed with the imperial court?”

Lu Yang was caught off guard. “Register?”

“Yes, according to the laws of the Great Xia Dynasty, any newly established organization must register with the local yamen. Those not registered are considered illegal operations and are subject to severe crackdowns.

“The former Four Great Diabolic Creeds, now the Three Great Diabolic Creeds, never registered.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Seeing Lu Yang and the others go quiet, he laughed heartily. “Alright, alright, out with it. Don’t give me all that flowery talk. What exactly is going on?”

As a member of the famous Dao-Seeking Nine, Fifth Elder naturally wasn’t taken in by Lu Yang’s bluff. What ancient immortal legacies? What support from prominent ancestral clans? Aren’t you just talking about yourselves?

After the destruction of the Everlasting Creed, Lu Yang obtained the legacy of the Everlasting Immortal.

Since Meng Jingzhou is the eldest son of the Meng Family, all the money he spends counts as support from a major ancestral clan.

Li Haoran’s incarnation in his past life, Qin Haoran, was a Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

Qin Yanyan’s father is Qin Haoran, so logically, she’s the first successor.

Lu Yang had no choice but to explain the whole situation honestly.

Fifth Elder clicked his tongue in amazement, his eyes shining. “You guys are something else, fabricating a non-existent Heavenly Court to deceive the Nine-Netherworlds Creed into forming an alliance. If you get lucky, you might even find the Radiant Sun Creed and the Heartless Creed.” A reminiscent expression emerged on his visage. “Back in the day, the nine of us did something similar.”

“What did you do?” Lu Yang and the other three looked at Fifth Elder, curiosity gnawing at their hearts.

Fifth Elder picked up a stone and casually refined it into a table and chairs, inviting Lu Yang and the others to sit.

The table and chairs appeared thin, but after being refined by Fifth Elder, an artifact-refining grandmaster, they were sturdy enough to withstand several attacks from a Golden Core cultivator.

Fifth Elder continued with his story. “It was probably nine hundred years ago. Eighth Junior Brother disguised himself as a low-level cultivator as he went out to carry out heroic and chivalrous deeds. By chance, he discovered the traces of a Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower. Instead of exposing him, Eighth Junior Brother yielded to his nature and consorted with that follower, indulging in debauchery and gambling day and night. Most of the time, Eighth Junior Brother paid for everything. His behavior quickly earned the trust of that Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower.”

Although Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou hadn’t interacted much with Eighth Elder, they had an indelible impression of him. After all, Eighth Elder had dared to sell Meng Jingzhou the sect’s entrance exam questions from twenty years ago, even vowing that they were the real deal.

“What happened next?”

“That Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower asked how Eighth Junior Brother got so many spirit stones despite being fellow Nascent Soul cultivators. Eighth Junior Brother explained that his organization had unearthed a longevity pill formula. Although the effects weren’t significant, it was enough to drive cultivators nearing the end of their lives into a frenzied fight to lay their hands on it.

“Eighth Junior Brother also stressed that this was insider information from their organization, saying, ‘If we didn’t get along so well, I wouldn’t even share this with you.’

“However, the production of the longevity pill formula was too low to meet demand. They needed a large amount of spirit stones to purchase raw materials and scale up production.

“Eighth Junior Brother expressed that their organization was short on funds and asked that follower if he could lend them some money. It wouldn’t be a free loan. He promised they would return the principal plus twenty percent interest after a year.

“The Nine-Netherworlds Creed follower was tempted but still skeptical. At first, he only invested less than a hundred thousand spirit stones. A year later, Eighth Junior Brother returned the principal on time, along with the twenty percent interest.

“That follower tested it for three years, and it worked every year.

“Eventually, that follower’s superior in the Nine-Netherworlds Creed found out about it and also wanted to invest. He asked Eighth Junior Brother if it was possible, and Eighth Junior Brother replied that he needed to consult his superior. Then, he brought Ninth Brother in, in other words, your shifu.

“Your shifu said it was possible to invest, and that superior invested for five years. He more than doubled his assets and was over the moon.

“However, wind passes through all walls; no secret can stay hidden forever. This matter ultimately reached the ears of the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. The creed leader didn’t tell anyone and instead cautiously requested to observe the pill-concocting process. Thus, Old Eight and Old Nine called us over to stage a fake scene, with Eldest Brother posing as the person consuming the pill.

“After the visit, the creed leader felt that the nine of us were quite reliable, so he invested his own spirit stones and earned a lot of money.

“That said, it was not enough for him, so he set his sights on the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s treasury, using it for investment. Once the profits rolled in a year later, the treasury’s spirit stones would be restored in full, and the interest would go straight into his own pocket—wouldn’t that be perfect?

“By shifting part of the treasury’s funds, the creed leader raked in even more money, but he was still unsatisfied. In the end, he decided he might as well invest most of the funds.

“Then we ran off with the money.

Lu Yang had once believed the same, but after learning about the Qilin Immortal’s existence from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he saw through the lie. Only then did he realize that what seemed like ordinary knowledge to him, such as the titles of the Four Ancient Immortals, was something even Fusion cultivators rarely knew. Even the long-lived Little Herb Kings were unaware.

Could the Everlasting Immortal Fairy really be my golden finger cheat?

“The Qilin Immortal is the sole true qilin in the world and the only immortal among the demons. As for you, the Qilin Immortality Herbs...”

The Qilin Immortality Herb asked eagerly, “How did we come to be?”

“The blood of the Qilin Immortal dripped onto a spirit plant. Influenced by the immortal blood, it took on the form of a qilin.”

The Qilin Immortality Herb immediately felt its status elevate and straightened its stem proudly.

Lu Yang was floored. “The Qilin Immortal could still get injured after becoming an immortal? Who was the enemy?”

Could it be that there were terrifying beings in the ancient era that threatened even the ancient immortals? Is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy worried about my low cultivation and keeping it from me, waiting until I grow stronger to reveal the truth?

The Immortal Fairy had the best of intentions and put in much effort, but unfortunately, I still detected subtle clues! Should I pretend not to know, or should I keep pressing for answers?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was also baffled. “I wasn’t there at the time, so I don’t know the details. It happened during the Qilin Immortal’s wedding. Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other two immortals beat up the Qilin Immortal, causing him to bleed profusely.

“Why would they fight on such a joyous day? I don’t understand them. Is this what they call ‘bridal chamber hijinks?’”[1]

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, weren’t you the one who sparked trouble at the wedding with an immortal fruit? That led to a cooking competition between the Dragon and Phoenix prodigies, who were culinary masters under your tutelage. The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other two immortals served as judges to appraise the dishes. Afterward, they thought the Qilin Immortal was the source of the trouble and gave him a beating.

So that’s when the Qilin Immortality Herb came into existence. This Qilin Immortality Herb in the herb garden is probably a descendant of that original one.

“A battle between immortals?” The Dao Enlightenment Tree and the Ginseng Doll gasped, surprised that one could still meet with mishaps even after becoming an immortal in the ancient era.

Based on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words, they automatically conjured up a scene in their minds.

In the ancient era, during the Qilin Immortal’s wedding, countless demons gathered to pay their respects. The three immortals who were enemies of the Qilin Immortal deliberately chose this joyous occasion to provoke him. For the sake of his beautiful wives and dignity, he unleashed his wrath and faced the three immortals without fear. He valiantly took action and stirred up monstrous waves with his supreme immortal power, shocking all the ages!

This battle defended his unparalleled status as the only immortal among the demons!

The fact that an immortal bled was a testament to how brutal that battle was!

A bona fide immortal battle!

This Everlasting Immortal Fairy truly doesn’t treat us as outsiders. With just a casual remark, she revealed a glimpse into the ancient secrets.

They turned their gazes to Lu Yang.

Lu Yang has followed the Immortal Fairy all this while. How many ancient secrets must he have learned? And how many cruel ancient battles has he heard about?

Chapter 323: Qilin Immortal, I’ve Remembered You!

“By the way, this is the soil I found—Xirang Soil.”[1] The Qilin Immortality Herb snapped out of its astonishment from hearing the tale of an immortal battle and remembered why it had come here.

“Xirang Soil? The legendary immortal soil that can block rivers with just a small lump?!” Lu Yang had read about this precious soil in books. Its effects were so mystical that it was revered as “immortal soil” by people.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy circled the clump of Xirang Soil a few times and recognized its origins. “Ah, this is good stuff the Nine-Layers Immortal created. It expands when it comes into contact with water and is used for managing river floods.

“Back then, the river channels were a mess, and inundation from the rivers was common. Furthermore, tribes settled along the rivers, making the riverbanks the most densely populated areas. This meant that every time the rivers flooded, it would cause massive casualties, and post-disaster reconstruction was also challenging.

“Large tribes were mostly fine; they had powerful cultivators controlling the river flow with Water Control Techniques, keeping their tribes out of danger. However, small and medium-sized tribes bore the brunt of the disaster. The cultivation levels of their cultivators weren’t sufficient to control the massive rivers.

“Although the Nine-Layers Immortal was born in the Lianshan Clan, the largest human tribe, he treated everyone equally and was kind to the smaller tribes as well. After he became an immortal, he focused on solving the flooding problem and created a type of soil that expands upon contact with water—the Xirang Soil you’re holding.

“Oh, by the way, Lu Yang, you can’t eat the Xirang Soil,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy reminded him.

“Is there a problem with it?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang with pity. “Xirang Soil expands when it comes into contact with water, and that also applies to saliva. If you eat a mouthful of Xirang Soil, it will expand until it wraps around you.”

“Forget it then.” Lu Yang swiftly backed away from the Xirang Soil.

The Three-Leaf Starry Herb and the Time Terminus Flower brought two other types of rare soil. Lu Yang tried them one by one, but none of them showed any effect.

“It doesn’t work.” It can’t be that all three types of soil are about improving one’s constitution.

“Why don’t you take a few more bites?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy refused to believe it.

Lu Yang polished off all the soil the Little Herb Kings had brought, but there was still no change.

He wondered if he hadn’t eaten enough, so he asked the Little Herb Kings to find more soil. With that, he kept eating until dawn but still felt no change.

“Immortal Fairy, is your Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth even reliable?” Lu Yang began to suspect that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been playing with him.

“How can it be unreliable? This is the taotie’s mighty ability the Qilin Immortal taught me!”

An ominous feeling crept into Lu Yang. “Wait, the Qilin Immortal taught it to you?”

“That’s right.”

“When did he teach it to you? Was it after his wedding?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was astonished. “How did you know that?

“Not long after the wedding, the Qilin Immortal came to me and asked if I wanted to learn an ancient mighty ability of the Taotie Tribe. I said it wouldn’t hurt to learn one.

“Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth wasn’t hard to learn. I picked it up quickly. After mastering it, the Qilin Immortal asked if I wanted to try eating dirt. I said, ‘I’m already an immortal. What use would eating dirt be?’

“Hearing that, he left in disappointment.”

Lu Yang was silent for a long while before tentatively asking, “Immortal Fairy, you mentioned earlier that you had read about the Taotie Tribe’s story in books. Did those books state that eating dirt can improve one’s cultivation talent?”

“No, that’s what the Qilin Immortal told me.”

Lu Yang, “...”

He finally painted a rough picture of what had happened. Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth was indeed for eating dirt, and the Taotie Tribe did start out by eating dirt. But there was never any mention of eating dirt to improve one’s cultivation talent!

The Qilin Immortal wanted to get back at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, so he purposely taught her this mighty ability and used the claim of “improving one’s cultivation talent” to pique her curiosity, hoping she would eat dirt. That way, he could spread the word about the Immortal Fairy eating dirt and mock her.

Who would have thought that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s seeming naivety masked great wisdom—she didn’t fall for it at all!

Three hundred thousand years later, an unlucky guy walked into the Qilin Immortal’s pit trap and spent the whole night eating dirt—me.

Qilin Immortal, since you couldn’t trick the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, you tricked me instead, huh? I’ve remembered you!

~~~

When everyone arrived at the meeting point, there were still no signs of Lu Yang.

Just as they were about to go look for him, they saw him walking over with laborious steps, his face the color of dirt.

Meng Jingzhou was startled by Lu Yang’s appearance. “What happened to you? Did you fall into a mud pit while sleeping?”

Lu Yang acted as if nothing had happened and waved his hand. “It’s nothing, just a minor setback while learning a mighty ability. It’s common on the path of cultivation.”

Fortunately, Golden Core cultivators didn’t need to sleep, or else Lu Yang would be too exhausted to even open his eyes.

Fifth Elder was very worried about Lu Yang. “Are you really fine?”

“Really, I’m fine.”

“That’s good then.”

Fifth Elder took out a flying shuttle from his sleeve and gently tossed it into the air. The flying shuttle was enlarged to the size of a merchant guild’s flying vessel. As it opened, it revealed seats and various sophisticated amenities inside.

This was Fifth Elder’s favorite flying magical treasure. In terms of construction cost, it was far more expensive than a flying vessel.

“Get on.”

After everyone hopped onto the flying shuttle one after another, it closed.

“Everyone seated and buckled up?” Fifth Elder stood at the front and asked calmly.

Despite not understanding his intention, everyone obediently sat in their seats and replied in unison that they were ready.

“That’s good then.” Fifth Elder nodded.

He raised his index and middle fingers, activating the flying shuttle. As it rapidly accelerated, it pierced through the sound barrier with a deafening boom.

It felt like a crushing weight was pressing down on them, forcing everyone to stay glued to their seats. Lu Yang couldn’t move an inch. No matter how hard he gritted his teeth, strained his neck, and used every ounce of his strength, he was unable to break free. He could do nothing but stick to his seat. Despite attempting to form a spirit energy barrier around himself for protection, at such a speed, the spirit energy shattered as soon as it left his body, making it impossible to maintain the barrier.

Finally, the pressure disappeared. The four of them leaned forward, their arms resting on their legs and their heads drooping as they stabilized themselves. They felt a sense of relief wash over them, as if they had narrowly escaped disaster. They hadn’t even felt this way when facing the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

Fifth Elder paced in front of the four and lectured, “I deliberately accelerated just now to train your ability to react to sudden situations. Remember that feeling. As cultivators, you must always be alert to potential dangers around you.

“When I was young, I often raced flying vessels and had to deal with law enforcement cultivators coming from who knows where. But not once did they manage to catch me.“

The four of them looked at Fifth Elder warily.

Right now, the biggest danger is you!

The flying vessel flew at an incredible speed. Just as Lu Yang wanted to show off his newly acquired “Swallowing Heaven,” Fifth Elder announced, “We’re here.”

Meng Jingzhou looked down and saw Yanjiang Commandery.

The flying shuttle hovered directly above Yanjiang Commandery, completely invisible to the naked eye.

“Let’s go down.”

The four of them exchanged glances with one another. They searched around but couldn’t find any equipment for descending.

Only Golden Core cultivators could fly. Li Haoran and Qin Yanyan weren’t at the Golden Core Stage yet, and Lu Yang was afraid of heights.

How are we supposed to get down?

Fifth Elder slapped his forehead. “I’ll take you down.”

Fifth Elder waved his sleeve, and before Lu Yang could register what was happening, everything went black. When he struggled to open his eyes, he found himself lying on the floor of the barbeque shop, with Li Haoran lying to his left and Qin Yanyan lying to his right.

“What happened? Is Fifth Elder also capable of Sleeve Cosmos?” Lu Yang was surprised. Isn’t it supposed to be an extremely difficult mighty ability to master?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy said faintly, “No, he simply knocked you out and carried you here.”

Chapter 324: The Barbeque Shop Reopens

After Lu Yang woke, Li Haoran and Qin Yanyan also gradually came to. The father and daughter duo scanned their surroundings, confused about the situation.

“All awake?” Fifth Elder sat on a stool, his demeanor as serene as the wind and clouds.

Qin Yanyan recalled the moment before they passed out. Fifth Elder had waved his sleeve, and everything went black. When they regained consciousness, they were already here.

It’s exactly like the legendary Sleeve Cosmos!

“I know! You just used Sleeve Cosmos, right?!” Qin Yanyan exclaimed excitedly, not expecting to experience such a legendary mighty ability firsthand. As expected of an elder from the Dao-Seeking Sect!

Fifth Elder showed a faint smile, and his silence spoke volumes, as if an unspoken understanding passed between them.

Li Haoran wore a thoughtful expression. I haven’t heard that Shifu knows Sleeve Cosmos.

Having observed everything throughout this whole time, Meng Jingzhou raised an eyebrow. He was the only one among the four who hadn’t passed out.

After knocking out Lu Yang and the other two, Fifth Elder had convinced himself that it was because he was worried about their fear of heights and lack of flying experience. It might be too much for them to handle if they jumped down directly. Better to knock them out and carry them—it’s a lot more convenient.

Then, Fifth Elder pulled out three sacks, stuffed the three of them inside, and carried them off with a practiced ease that suggested he had done this many times before.

“So this is the One More Time Barbeque Shop you mentioned?” Before setting off, Fifth Elder had done his homework. He had asked Dai Bufan for the mission report by Lu Yang and the others, thereby learning what had happened in Yanjiang Commandery.

As Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou gazed at the familiar setup, nostalgia spread across their expressions. Time shuttles past, the world shifts, and people have changed. In the blink of an eye, so many years have flown by, and even the Everlasting Creed has been destroyed. Who would have thought that we could return here?

Fifth Elder brushed his hand across the table, wiping off a thick layer of dust. “Three months have passed. It’s time to clean up.”

Just as Lu Yang and the other three juniors were about to start cleaning, they saw Fifth Elder wave his hand. “No need for such trouble.” His lips quivered slightly as he muttered an incantation no one could hear clearly, then casually flicked out a seal.

The seal landed on the ground, and the space seemed to tremble, sending out invisible ripples that spread in circles. The dust on the tables, chairs, and floor began to undulate with the spatial ripples, peeling off from the surfaces and diffusing outward. Even the dust on Lu Yang and the other three shook slightly and left them.

Once all the dust, grease, and other filth had dispersed to the corners, a suction force appeared in Fifth Elder’s palm, pulling the muck inward and forming a vortex. Finally, the dirt and grime condensed into a ball. Fifth Elder clenched his fist, and the ball of nastiness vanished without a trace.

The barbeque shop felt brand new, as if everything had just been replaced.

“This is the Dust-Cleansing Incantation. It is often used for cleaning and maintaining hygiene. In your spare time, you can pick up these practical little spells,” Fifth Elder explained. “If you find someone unpleasant to the eye, you can also use the Dust-Cleansing Incantation to gather filth into a ball and throw it at them.”

This was Fifth Elder’s original motivation for learning the Dust-Cleansing Incantation.

“Time to reopen our shop!”

Lu Yang whipped out various seasonings, skewers, and an Automatic Skewering Array from his identity jade tablet. Items like barbeque grills were available in the shop, untouched since they left.

“This Automatic Skewering Array is quite interesting. Very innovative.” With just a glance, Fifth Elder deduced the function of the array.

Lu Yang answered inwardly, Of course. This is the latest achievement of the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups, combining the wisdom of four Fusion cultivators.

Fifth Elder asked, “Is there an automatic barbecue array or magical treasure?”

Lu Yang shook his head. It hasn’t been designed yet.

“Hmm, in that case, I’ll design it. But I’ve never barbecued before, so I’ll need to practice for a few days to figure out how to design an automatic barbecue magical treasure.”

What Fifth Elder enjoyed the most was crafting magical treasures that never existed before.

Lu Yang was delighted. I was wondering whether I should capture a couple of tiger-henchman ghosts, but it seems unnecessary now.

He mixed the seasonings in specific ratios and soon produced a jar of reddish barbeque sauce with a Barbarian Tribe twist.

“I’ll go out and buy some ingredients first,” Lu Yang said, leaving Fifth Elder to try his hand at barbeque.

Lu Yang pushed the door open, drawing surprised looks from passers-by on the street.

“Shop Manager Lu!”

“What? This is Shop Manager Lu?”

“Is the barbeque shop reopening?”

“I heard Manager Lu went out to start his own business. Did he fail in his venture and return to run the barbeque shop again?”

“Wasn’t it said that Manager Lu went home to inherit his family business? Why is he back?”

“There’s such a story?”

“Haven’t you heard? Manager Lu got separated from his parents when he was young. The barbeque recipe was a childhood memory of his. A formidable figure came here to eat skewers, and after finishing his meal, he was moved to tears, saying that only someone from his family could produce such a flavor. He asked who made it, leading to a reunion between father and son. After that, the barbeque shop closed.”

“Why did I hear that Manager Lu had a wealthy fiancée who took him away?”

The passers-by chatted among themselves. One More Time Barbeque Shop was the most popular in Yanjiang Commandery; even neighboring commanderies and counties had heard of it.

Unfortunately, after the Spring Harvest Festival, the shop closed, and people missed the food terribly. They even came up with all sorts of theories about Lu Yang’s departure.

As for the death of the commandery governor, no one would connect it to the barbeque shop, especially since it was adorned with commendation silk banners.

“Manager Lu, is the barbeque shop reopening?”

“Exactly! Not eating your skewers at night feels like something’s missing!”

Faced with the fervent crowd, Lu Yang raised his hand and announced loudly, “Everyone, calm down! We’ve returned to reopen the barbeque shop. Please rest assured. Our initial plan is to reopen tomorrow!”

“Great!”

After finally breaking free from the crowd, Lu Yang was surrounded again at the market. By the time he arrived back at the barbeque shop, he was panting and felt that going out was more exhausting than fighting.

“I’m back!”

Lu Yang tossed the meat and vegetables onto the Automatic Skewering Array. It automatically cut the ingredients into small pieces, and wooden skewers floated up, threading the meat and vegetables together. The process was fairly smooth.

Fifth Elder carried the skewers to the grill and turned his head around to ask, “Do you have a special flame for barbecuing?” As an artifact-refining grandmaster, he wielded seven types of true fire, but they were all too intense, suitable only for forging artifacts but not for barbequing.

“I have Three Flavor True Fire!” Lu Yang volunteered himself. My true fire is perfect for barbecuing.

“I have true fire too,” Meng Jingzhou said, a searing flame ignited from his palm.

“Pure Yang True Fire?” Fifth Elder recognized the flame in Meng Jingzhou’s palm. Every cultivator with a Single’s Spirit Root would automatically wield this true fire after forming their golden core.

“But your flame isn’t as effective as Lu Yang’s Three Flavor True Fire, right?”

Meng Jingzhou flashed a confident smile. “No, my Pure Yang True Fire is the product of the Dual Single’s Golden Core. It has effects that previous Pure Yang True Fire didn’t possess.”

Fifth Elder was curious. “What is it?”

“It can boost one’s yang virility.

“Any ingredient cooked with the Pure Yang True Flame can boost one’s yang virility!”

Chapter 325: The Non-Suspicious Barbeque Shop

Fifth Elder inhaled sharply. Based on this effect alone, the Pure Yang True Fire can already rank first among the 108 True Fires.

The 108 True Fires had different functions each. Some flames were weak, unable to kill even mortals, yet they were highly effective at burning space. On the other hand, some flames were powerful but were difficult to control and prone to explosions. There were also flames that didn’t burn the body but only the soul. For these reasons, it was hard to rank the various types of true fire, much less definitively determine a first or second place.

But if you claim that your true fire can boost one’s yang virility...

I can’t speak for others, but I will definitely cast a vote for the Pure Yang True Fire.

“Let me study it and see if your Pure Yang True Fire can be stabilized into a fire seed.

“And your Three Flavor True Fire, let me study that too.”

Fifth Elder asked for Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s true fires and worked on forming them into fire seeds that could burn continuously. Otherwise, every time they barbecued, they would need Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to infuse spirit energy to light the flames. What would be the point of an automated barbecue grill then?

“The best approach is to combine the two flames,” Fifth Elder mused, not expecting to face such a challenge so soon after arriving in Yanjiang Commandery.

“You can combine two flames?” Qin Yanyan asked in surprise. She had never heard of such a theory before.

“It’s possible,” Fifth Elder replied without looking up. “In history, there have been people who fused two, three, or even more flames together and hurled them at enemies. The power was astonishing, and it was an effective means of challenging opponents beyond one’s level.

“Alright, all of you, get out. I’ll research this myself.” Fifth Elder shooed the four of them out like they were little chicks.

Three formidable cultivators descended upon Yanjiang Commandery. They concealed their auras and blended into the crowd, disguising themselves as traveling merchants passing through.

The three of them entered a private room in a restaurant and set up an array to block external probing methods. Only then did they feel safe enough to remove their disguises.

The visitors were none other than Shi Huagu, the vice creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, and his two subordinates. One of them was Huo Huashen, the Nascent Soul cultivator who had brought Qin Haoran’s debt note to Shi Huagu. His parents had named him Huo Huashen in the hopes that his cultivation would reach the Divine Transfiguration Stage.[1]

Shi Huagu lifted the curtain of the private room. Through the window, he could see One More Time Barbeque Shop diagonally across the street. It was now night, and the barbeque shop was bustling, a long line already forming outside.

“So many people?” Shi Huagu was stunned. Since the barbeque shop is a liaison point for the Heavenly Court Creed, shouldn’t it be as low-key as possible? Is this a case of acting the exact opposite of what one would expect, or is it a display of the Heavenly Court Creed’s strength, that they are unafraid of being detected by the righteous path?

“Roger!” the two of them chorused in unison before vanishing from the private room.

Not long after, Shi Huagu walked out of the private room. The waiter presented the bill to him. “Dear guest, your two friends have already left. About the payment...”

Shi Huagu’s face darkened. Shouldn’t my subordinates have fought to pay the bill for me?

Shi Huagu lowered his head pensively. “It’s possible that the Heavenly Court Creed wanted to get in touch with the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups through the Yanjiang Branch, but before they could establish contact, the Everlasting Creed was annihilated by the Dao-Seeking Sect. What a pity.”

His subordinates’s report went on. “Based on our analysis, four months ago, the cultivation level Little Manager Lu displayed was at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage, but it’s unclear whether that was a disguise or if he was truly at that cultivation stage and only recently reached the Golden Core Stage.”

“Oh well. Since there’s nothing suspicious about the barbeque shop, let’s pay it a visit and see whether the waters are deep or shallow!”

Chapter 326: Three Visits to the Barbeque Shop

“I heard there’s a barbeque shop in Yanjiang Commandery that can boost one’s yang virility. This is the one?”

~~~

“What a booming business!” Shi Huagu finally understood the true scale of the shop’s popularity now that he stood before its entrance rather than observing it from a distance.

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed operated many businesses, but none attracted crowds of this magnitude.

The line stretched from their entrance all the way to the neighboring shop’s doorway, completely blocking it. However, the neighboring shop didn’t mind—impatient customers would visit their shop instead, making their business even better than before.

Huo Huashen transmitted an auditory message. “Apparently, this shop used to offer delivery but discontinued it because they can’t even handle the dine-in customers now.

Shi Huagu snorted coldly and prepared to barge right into the shop. “Have you forgotten who we are? Why do we have to wait in line?”

Two Divine Transfiguration cultivators and one Fusion cultivator—this lineup is already enough to establish a second-class sect. Even first-class sects have to receive us with respect.

This is a mere barbeque shop. It’s not like it’s the headquarters of the Heavenly Court Creed.

“There are people cutting the line here!”

“Hey! You three got no manners?!”

“Uncivilized!”

Chapter 330: The Cultivation of Our Creed Leader and Yun Zhi of the Dao-Seeking Sect Are Evenly Matched

Shi Huagu was utterly astonished. Even Huo Huashen, who had been maintaining his aloof expert facade, could no longer keep up the act.

The barbeque shop’s business spoke for itself, with the demand far outstripping the supply. It was more profitable than robbing money. The line of customers outside after closing time was a testament to the shop’s overwhelming popularity.

As a Fusion expert, Shi Huagu had tasted every delicacy in the world, including dishes superior to these skewers. They were made from ingredients so rare that they couldn’t be purchased with mere spirit stones.

Yet, the ingredients used by this barbeque shop can be found in any market. Despite the ordinary ingredients, their food can be sold at premium prices. Just imagine how astronomical the profit margins must be!

The profits from a single barbeque shop would normally not interest a Divine Transfiguration or Fusion cultivator. But what if they opened branches across the entire Central Continent? The potential profits would be staggering enough to tempt anyone.

Of course, the most crucial factor is my debt of one billion. If I fail to repay it, I’ll have to get struck by lightning every month. Now’s the time I need money the most!

Most importantly, their business is legitimate and fears no investigations, unlike the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. We basically have no legitimate businesses. The only quasi-legitimate business is probably our funeral services.

However, funeral services can also be dangerous. Once, a higher-up in the creed who specialized in refining corpses suddenly had a spark of an idea to dig up the clients’ buried family members for refinement. Later, the families somehow caught wind of it and immediately reported us.

Luckily, our creed acted decisively, disavowing that idiot and severing all ties with him.

Fusion tiger-henchman ghosts? This is the highest known cultivation among them. Only someone a major realm higher can refine and subjugate these tiger-henchman ghosts.

Chapter 331: Pleasant Cooperation

Chapter 332: He Dares Claim That He’s the Fastest With This?

The flying shuttle traveled a hundred times slower than the first time they rode it. In Fifth Elder’s words, he wanted to let Lu Yang and the others “enjoy the scenery in the sky.”

Even so, the flying shuttle still overtook flying vessel after flying vessel, its speed so fast that Lu Yang and the other three shuddered in fear, too terrified to even glance at the view outside.

Lu Yang waved his hand confidently. “No need for that. I just learned a primitive mighty ability, which can gather all the spirit qi in the surroundings. It can replace the Spirit-Qi Gathering Array.”

Fifth Elder was stunned. I never knew such a mighty ability existed. Did Yun Zhi teach him?

Proudly tilting his head back, Lu Yang opened his mouth and unleashed the primitive mighty ability of the Taotie Tribe—Swallowing Heaven.

Instantly, spirit qi surged toward them in an endless stream, increasing the density of spirit qi around them.

This mighty ability hardly consumes any spirit energy and is much cheaper than a Spirit-Qi Gathering Array while providing comparable effects. The only downside is that it looks somewhat undignified. Tipping your head backward with your mouth wide open like a divine dog howling at the moon[1] isn’t exactly elegant.
