Originally, he shouldn’t have awakened now. According to the plan, the Imperial Preceptor would rouse them up one by one. Unfortunately, his slumber place was discovered by a few reckless cultivators, who even thought that they had stumbled upon a great fortuitous opportunity and fervently dug into the site, ultimately disturbing his slumber.

In a moment of rage, he slaughtered those cultivators on the spot.

Unexpectedly, his actions alerted the local chief constable. Noting his aggressiveness, the chief constable immediately contacted his superiors, and the imperial capital dispatched two Fusion cultivators to apprehend him.

And the reason for the arrest was even the ridiculous crime of culpable homicide. As an almighty Fusion cultivator, what’s killing a few insignificant cultivators? It was clearly just an excuse to arrest me.

From his perspective, the Great Yu Dynasty was at its zenith. He believed the so-called Great Dynasty to be a bunch of usurpers shamelessly claiming legitimacy to the throne.

Fortunately, I had prepared contingencies to restore myself to my peak for a short time. Moreover, I specialize in escape techniques. Eluding pursuit will be effortless.

As expected of the Imperial Preceptor.

Notwithstanding that, the Imperial Preceptor had maintained that no dynasty lasted for eternity. Even the formidable ancient era had met its end. No matter how strong the Great Yu Dynasty was, it couldn’t surpass the ancient era with the Four Ancient Immortals.

The Great Yu Dynasty would not last forever.

Therefore, there was only one way for the Great Yu Dynasty to continue its legacy—awaken in the new dynasty and leverage the Battle of the Great Battle to rebuild the Great Yu Dynasty, sustaining its fortune!

He shook his head, setting aside these thoughts for now. His current priority was to lose his two pursuers.

“Old Chu, keep chasing him first. I’ll find some reinforcements.”

Old Chu didn’t understand what his partner was trying to do. Isn’t it too late to find reinforcements now? Nevertheless, he trusted his partner’s judgement and nodded. “Alright.”

Our savior!

Since this constable, Yu Qian, is from the same generation as him, his cultivation can’t be too low. Even if he is a constable, he must be a big shot in the imperial city, maybe someone like a chief constable.

When Fifth Elder raced flying shuttles in his youth, it had caused much trouble for Yu Qian and others. The reason Yu Qian could run so fast now was precisely due to his training from chasing Fifth Elder back then.

“You can’t just say that. When did I race again? Do you have evidence?” freewebnovel.com

Yu Qi was so irked that he wanted to hit him. You raced so fast that even recording orbs couldn’t capture your flying shuttle’s shadow! How could there be any evidence?

Chapter 333: You High-Level Cultivators Truly Have Many Fancy Tricks

“By the way, I’m now with the Luoshui Guard, no longer a constable,” Yu Qian mentioned.

“Oh, that explains it. Chasing ancient era cultivators doesn’t really fall under the responsibility of constables now.” Fifth Elder was unsurprised; rather, he was more focused on when he could catch up to the Great Yu cultivator.

“What’s the Luoshui Guard?” Lu Yang barely managed to communicate with Meng Jingzhou with his spiritual consciousness. His knowledge of the Great Xia Dynasty’s official positions was nowhere near as extensive as Meng Jingzhou’s.

Li Haoran and Qin Yanyan also listened curiously through their spiritual consciousness. Qin Yanyan had heard snippets from her mother, but it could not be compared to Meng Jingzhou’s depth of knowledge.

Meng Jingzhou explained, “The Luoshui Guard is a special organization established by the Great Xia Dynasty. They specialize in apprehending malevolent cultivators, such as diabolic creed members, bullies who abuse their power, and ancient cultivators who don’t follow the rules.

Fifth Elder and Yu Qian were unfazed, still in the mood for chatter.

Yu Qian was not anxious. If even Fifth Elder can’t catch up, it’s futile no matter how hard I try.

“By the way, you don’t have to show him mercy when we catch up. He’s a murderer.”

“Such audacity!” Fifth Elder’s temper flared. With a stomp, he erupted in cyan flames, and the flying shuttle’s speed increased twofold further.

The Great Yu cultivator suddenly sensed impending catastrophe. Turning his head around, he saw a flying shuttle wreathed in cyan flames barreling straight at him.

“What in the world is that?!” His expression shifted drastically. This flying shuttle is too fast. I’d believe it even if you told me that a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator is chasing me.

The incredible speed of the flying shuttle gave him no time to react. Its razor-sharp prow collided into his chest.

The flying vessel was a flying magical treasure meticulously crafted by Fifth Elder. It was firm and nigh-indestructible. Combined with its speed that almost rivaled that of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, one could easily imagine its destructive power.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

The flying shuttle crashed through three mountains successively before getting stuck on the fourth mountain peak, sending dust swirling through the air.

Old Chu, the Luoshui Guard trailing behind, widened his eyes in a daze. “This is Zhou Xin’s flying shuttle!”

“Trying to compete with me in speed?” Fifth Elder let out a cold grunt as he jumped off the flying shuttle.

He had purposely held back, keeping the Great Yu cultivator alive. The latter had a gaping hole in his chest and coughed up blood as he struggled to activate the power of the ‘Rules.’

<I hereby set a rule: these mountains shall transform into mountain gods and obey my command...>

Yu Qian snorted and knocked him out with a punch. Trying to use the power of rules right in front of me? Do you think I’m here for decoration?

Old Chu rushed over. “Turns out it’s Elder Zhou Xin! No wonder Yu Qian wanted to seek reinforcements.” Upon seeing that the Great Yu cultivator was unconscious and bound in chains by Fifth Elder, he heaved a sigh of relief.

“Chu Dalong!” Fifth Elder had collaborated with the Luoshui Guard enough to recognize every Fusion member.

Old Chu’s face darkened. “How many times have I told you? My name is now Chu Long.”

Yu Qian cupped his fists in gratitude. “This scoundrel seems to hold some critical secrets. Many thanks for helping us capture him. Drinks are on me next time!”

“No need to thank me. It’s rare that I get to speed legally.” Fifth Elder was particularly pleased with his speeding experience this time. “Next time you encounter someone you can’t catch up to, just call me! I guarantee I’ll catch up to them!

“This chain has locked his powers. Consider a gift from my act of heroism.”

Though the Luoshui Guard had similar restraining methods, none were as effective as those crafted by an artifact-refining grandmaster like Fifth Elder.

Fifth Elder was kind enough to remind them, “By the way, since this guy is privy to pivotal secrets, for safety’s sake, it’s best to have a few more Fusion cultivators take him back. It’d be disastrous if he gets snatched away en route.”

“Agree, I’ll call for a few more people.” Yu Qian nodded and fired a talisman toward the sky.

Soon, two Fusion cultivators flew over. They also recognized Fifth Elder. After a brief exchange of greetings, the four Luoshui Guards escorted the Great Yu cultivator back to the court.

“Alright, time to go back. Matters related to archaic cultivators are not what you should get involved with now. It’s too dangerous. We can bring this up again when you have reached the Divine Transfiguration Stage.” Fifth Elder informed the four of them, advising them not to overthink.

As they prepared to leave, a few figures approached. Using earth-type spells, these people mended the craters in the mountains. Rocks and soil floated in the air, methodically filling the holes. Following that, they gathered the trees that were knocked down but still alive and replanted them with the Tree-Planting Mantra. As for those that had snapped, they were replaced with new trees.

“Who are these people?” Lu Yang and the others had never seen something like this.

Fifth Elder explained, “Oh, they’re sent by the court and in charge of dealing with the aftermath. Your current cultivation is not yet sufficient to cause such devastation. When your cultivation is higher, a few casual moves can perforate mountains, split the earth, and break off rivers.

“If left unchecked, the terrain here will experience changes daily, and in a few years, the Great Xia Dynasty will have to revise its maps. To prevent such situations, the Great Xia Dynasty recruited a group of cultivators specializing in repairing topography and proficient in earth- and wood-type spells.

“The capture today is considered an official affair, so I’m not liable for the damage to the mountains, and the court handles the aftermath. If it had stemmed from a private dispute, I would either have to repair the damaged terrain myself or hire someone with spirit stones to fix it.

“Hence, when your cultivation has reached a certain level, to avoid unnecessary trouble, you should fight on an arena stage or in the sky.

“Of course, if you’re fighting with diabolic cultivators, you’re not responsible for any destruction to the topography.

“In fact, the rule to repair the terrain after a battle traces back to an incident two hundred thousand years ago.

“Qing Province’s governor saw that the neighboring city was especially prosperous and began thinking about how he could make Qing Province equally prosperous. Since he happened to be at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he devised a brilliant plan and invited his good friend, also a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

“The two exchanged blows with great fanfare, altering the terrain during the process. Under the guise of their battle, they shifted the prosperous neighboring city into Qing Province’s territory.

“When the court learned of this matter, there was no applicable law, making it challenging to resolve. Therefore, they enacted a regulation stating that high-ranking cultivators must restore the landform to its original state after any battle.”

Lu Yang, “...”

You high-level cultivators truly have many fancy tricks.

Chapter 334: Li Haoran Forms His Golden Core

Lu Yang couldn’t help but feel that the Great Xia Dynasty truly had it rough. In his opinion, their legal system was already considerably comprehensive, with hardly any need to add or remove laws. It was sufficient to deal with any situation.

But cultivators simply have too many ideas.

That isn’t inherently problematic. After all, ideas alone don’t necessarily translate to reality. However, there will always be cultivators with overwhelming abilities to bring their ideas to life.

As a result, the legal system can never keep up with their antics. One example is the Qing Province’s governor that Fifth Elder mentioned.

It’s perfectly normal for Transcendent Tribulation cultivators to fight, right? It’s also perfectly normal for them to move mountains and fill the seas when fighting, right? Then, if I accidentally shift a neighboring city into Qing Province, that’s also perfectly normal, right?

What Lu Yang didn’t know was that the Dao-Seeking Nine used to make outstanding contributions to the Great Xia Dynasty’s legal code—mainly by exposing the many loopholes in their law.

“Fortunately, I’m an honest person who never causes trouble for the Great Xia Dynasty.” Lu Yang briefly glanced at Meng Jingzhou and Li Haoran, feeling a heavy weight of responsibility on his shoulders.

Why do I cultivate so assiduously to become number one? Isn’t it so that I can be a role model for them? And let them abide by the law like I do?

“Ex-dad, are you not feeling well?” Qin Yanyan noticed the sweat beading on Li Haoran’s forehead.

Li Haoran was trembling uncontrollably, his aura fluctuating wildly. It reached as low as the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage in one moment and reached as high as the Basic Golden Stage in the next.

Through gritted teeth, he forced out a few words. “I have an epiphany. I want to form my golden core.”

In a flash, Fifth Elder appeared right in front of Li Haoran. He scanned Li Haoran’s dantian with his spiritual consciousness and realized it was hazy—a telltale sign of his golden core condensing.

Fifth Elder said gravely, “Haoran, your situation is unique. As you are Qin Haoran’s reincarnation, you may meet unforeseen circumstances during your golden core formation process. Returning to the sect to form your golden core is the safest choice!”

Li Haoran rasped, “I’ll try. But my instinct is making my body go out of control. It already wants to form a golden core.”

Lu Yang had read about such cases in the books. This was the ideal scenario for Great Perfection Foundation Establishment cultivators. Their body would form a golden core spontaneously, and everything would fall in place naturally with no risk of failing. Moreover, it would guarantee at least an upper-third-grade golden core.

Such moments exemplified how one’s talent grew stronger with each reincarnation.

Unfortunately, there were too many uncertainties with Li Haoran, and everyone had a limited understanding of reincarnation. Forming his golden core here was not the preferred choice.

“Haoran, hang in there! I’ll steer the flying shuttle!” Fifth Elder flung open the hatch and whisked the four of them inside before hurtling forward at full speed.

“Deep breaths. Relax your body. Deep breaths. That’s right. Inhale...exhale...”

“Junior Brother Li, you have to hang in there! You and your golden core will definitely pull through!”

“Fifth Elder, slow down! Junior Brother Li is barely hanging on!”

“Junior Brother Li, relax. This is no big deal. Every cultivator has to go through this phase. Just push on a little more, and you’ll get through this.”

On the flying shuttle, two Golden Core “guardians,” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, attended to Li Haoran, offering encouragement, wiping his sweat, and tending to his every need.

Qin Yanyan, “...”

If I didn’t know better, I’d think you’re looking after a woman about to go into labor.

“The mist in the dantian is condensing. He’s about to form his golden core!“

”The embryonic form of the golden core has begun to show itself!”

“Junior Brother Li, jiayou! You’ve got this!”

Qin Yanyan found the uncanny resemblance even more striking now.

Li Haoran sat in the lotus position, absorbing the ambient spirit qi. The mist in his dantian reacted more violently, as waves of power swept across his entire body, including his skin, bones, and meridians.

As the mist continued to purify, it transformed into liquefied golden spirit energy. The golden spirit energy compressed once more, producing a flickering spark that devoured the surrounding spirit energy.

Finally, a full and plump golden core was formed.

Li Haoran had succeeded!

“I succeeded?” Li Haoran was slightly uncertain of himself. The process was fairly smooth, except for the two annoying “guardians” yammering in his ears.

“You’ve succeeded.” Fifth Elder nodded in confirmation after a thorough inspection. “But it’s still advisable that you return to the sect for a full examination.” He breathed a sigh of relief after checking that no anomalies had arisen before or after Li Haoran formed his golden core.

“I’ve finally formed a golden core.” Li Haoran also breathed a sigh of relief. At least Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou won’t be able to show off in front of me now.

“What kind of golden core did you form?”

Li Haoran laughed mischievously. “It’s an unprecedented golden core—the Rebirth Golden Core!”

“Rebirth Golden Core?!”

Lu Yang found the name of the golden core to be very grand. Rebirth Golden Core—does it mean that Li Haoran has comprehended the true meaning of reincarnation? Can he reincarnate with his memories intact and make up for his past regrets?

If that’s really the case, the title of his golden core may be fitting.

“Let me demonstrate.” Li Haoran lopped off his arm in one swift motion, causing everyone to recoil in fright. They wondered if there was something wrong with his head.

That was when a miraculous scene unfolded. The flesh at the severed area wriggled, and in the blink of an eye, a new arm had regrown.

“Limb rebirth and regeneration!”[1] Meng Jingzhou exclaimed. This is a spell many eunuchs dreamed of.

Lu Yang, “...”

So this is what you meant by “Rebirth Golden Core?”

That said, Limb Rebirth is quite useful in combat. Plus, judging by Li Haoran’s demonstration, it seems like regenerating a limb is an easy feat for him.

Compared to Meng Jingzhou’s Double Single’s Golden Core and Man Gu’s Ancestor Assembly Golden Core, Li Haoran’s Rebirth Golden Core is probably the most normal one in our cohort.

“It’s not just limbs. I can regenerate a new heart, blood, or even a head,” Li Haoran elucidated his ability with pride, while his severed arm was still twitching on the floor.

“Why did you suddenly form a golden core? Was it because you had some epiphany?” Meng Jingzhou thought back about what had happened before Li Haoran’s golden core formation. Only the court’s clean-up crew stood out.

He asked, “You wish to have a career in aftermath cleanup in the future?”

Li Haoran rolled his eyes, not knowing how he should react. “Of course not. It’s not like I know earth- and wood-type spells. It’s because I just obtained another fragment of Qin Haoran’s memories and felt it could be applied to my golden core formation. That was when I had an epiphany and was inspired to form my golden core.”

Meng Jingzhou was now even more curious. “What did you see in those memories?”

Li Haoran fell silent for a long while before slowly answering, “Relying on his ability to regenerate severed limbs, he sold blood.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou inhaled sharply. Truly a ruthless person.

While not as precious as Phoenix blood, a Fusion cultivator’s blood still commanded fairly high prices.

“The more Qin Haoran sold his blood, the more adept he became at Limb Rebirth. After obtaining these memories, I realized Limb Rebirth’s usefulness and applied it to the formation of my golden core.”

Fifth Elder stroked his beard in admiration. “To think Qin Haoran went so far for the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.”

Lu Yang shot Fifth Elder a sidelong glance. Weren’t you the ones who tricked the Nine-Netherworlds Creed into such poverty?

Lu Yang’s expression turned even stranger. “He sold blood before becoming creed leader.”

“Then why did he sell blood?”

“To earn money for visiting prostitutes.”

“He still couldn’t afford to visit prostitutes at the Fusion Stage?”

“He visited a lot.”

1. The Chinese term “chongsheng” can mean rebirth or to grow again. Considering the genre of “chongsheng” or rebirth, most people would assume he meant “rebirth.” ☜

Chapter 335: This Golden Core Can Sever Karma!

Although it was inappropriate to speak of a father’s visits to brothels in front of his daughter, the torment of reliving Qin Haoran’s memories left Li Haoran with no choice but to cast aside propriety and expose Qin Haoran’s sordid past.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou surreptitiously observed Qin Yanyan, noticing that she showed no signs of anger or disappointment.

Their actions didn’t go unnoticed by Qin Yanyan, who questioned them, “Why are you two looking at me? Did you think someone from a diabolic creed would be a good person? How could I not have anticipated something like this?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou pondered for a bit and found her reasoning sound.

It never occurred to these two that they themselves were from a diabolic creed.

Li Haoran began to narrate the tale. “Back then, Qin Haoran wasn’t the creed leader yet. He was the type to spend all his money as soon as he got it, never saving any. He lived by the philosophy of “if there is wine today, I’ll drink to my heart’s content,” enjoying the moment while it lasts.

“Thus, when he was broke, he often sold his body—specifically, his blood.

“Of course, he did take safety precautions. Before selling his blood, he would erase all traces of himself from it. After all, there were spells that could be cast through blood. Qin Haoran would avoid such potential issues.

“After the creed leader before him passed away from a fit of rage, Qin Haoran thought that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed had plenty of members and wealth. If he became the creed leader, wouldn’t that mean he could spend money however he pleased?

“Hence, he swept away all obstacles and defeated his competitors. After he finally became the creed leader, however, he discovered that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed wasn’t as wealthy as he’d imagined.

“But by then, it was too late to step down.”

Lu Yang could easily picture how desperate Qin Haoran must have felt.

After jubilantly taking on the mantle as creed leader, he dreamed of wielding absolute authority, commanding the wind and rain, and indulging in a life of debauchery where lakes of wine and forests of meat surrounded him. However, he discovered that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was so poor that it couldn’t even pay its followers their monthly stipends. Furthermore, the members below were oblivious to all this. Even if he announced the truth and proclaimed that the previous creed leader had lost the money in investments, people would simply assume that Qin Haoran had embezzled all the money himself.

“The previous creed leader scammed out of money? Impossible! We diabolic creeds have always been the ones scamming others. Since when did others scam us diabolic creeds?”

“Qin Haoran must be lying!”

Due to these sundry reasons, after Qin Haoran became the creed leader, he had no choice but to rectify his old habits and dutifully focus on developing...or rather, maintaining the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

Lu Yang suspected that the current Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader shared the same sentiments. “I thought becoming creed leader would be great, only to discover that it’s purely a burden. Whoever becomes creed leader must have been cursed to be unlucky for eight lifetimes.”

Moreover, the current creed leader can’t even speak the truth. Everyone would question, “When Qin Haoran was creed leader, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed could operate normally. Why is it that as soon as you take over the reins, you say that the creed has no money? Where has the money gone?”

Lu Yang wondered, How does the current creed leader make money? By following Qin Haoran’s example and taking out loans?

Li Haoran’s words interrupted Lu Yang’s thoughts. “Of course, Qin Haoran’s Limb Rebirth wasn’t just for selling blood. It could also block karma. But I’ve just formed my golden core, so I can’t use this move yet.”

“How so?” Lu Yang hadn’t expected Limb Rebirth to be related to something as profound as “karma.”

Li Haoran elaborated, “Think about. With Limb Rebirth, if your arm gets severed, can’t a new one grow back?”

“That’s right.” Lu Yang nodded.

“If your leg gets severed, can’t a new one grow back?”

“That’s right.” Meng Jingzhou nodded.

“Can’t your torso and internal organs also grow new ones back?”

“That’s right.” Qin Yanyan nodded.

“If your head gets severed, can’t a new one grow back?”

“That’s right.” Fifth Elder nodded.

Li Haoran revealed a sliver of a smile as he asked, “If a new head, torso, and limbs can grow new ones back, isn’t that equivalent to replacing the entire body?

“In that case, am I still the original me?”

Exclamation marks were practically everywhere in the air.

“If my whole body has been replaced and I’m no longer the original me, can karma still find me?”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, Truly a ruthless individual who could become the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. Who could have thought of a skill like this?

“However, this involves karma after all. My cultivation realm isn’t stable yet, but once it stabilizes, I might be able to achieve this too.”

Li Haoran found his golden core to be pretty good. Not only can it help me in battle, but it can also efface karma, truly living up to the name “rebirth.”

~~~

As they spoke, the flying shuttle returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Fifth Elder took Li Haoran to meet the other elders and Yun Zhi to check if there were any issues with his golden core formation.

“Junior Brother Lu, Junior Brother Meng, Senior Brother Dai is looking for you,” a senior male disciple informed the two upon seeing them. frёeweɓηovel.coɱ

The two were caught off guard. “He’s looking for us?”

We didn’t do anything bad on this trip, right?

“Niece, stay at Hundred Refinements Peak for now. We need to step away briefly.” Lu Yang told Qin Yanyan to cultivate at Hundred Refinements Peak or explore the place and experience the Dao-Seeking Sect’s culture while waiting for them.

Best that she visits the dining hall.

~~~

The two arrived at the Great Mission Hall.

“Senior Brother Dai, you were looking for us?

“Fifth Elder accompanied us on this trip. We didn’t do anything out of line!” Lu Yang quickly declared that he was innocent.

Dai Bufan breathed a sigh of relief. “That’s good then. Every time you two go out, you get embroiled in a heap of issues. I’m worried that one day you will somehow be close to wiping out the diabolic creeds, and I would still be in the dark about everything you had done.”

As Dai Bufan managed the Dao-Seeking Sect’s intelligence network in First Elder’s stead, whenever Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou returned from a trip, their exploits would force Dai Bufan to reorganize the sect’s intelligence.

I’m worried that someday these two will cheerfully come to me and report, “Senior Brother Dai, great news! We have gotten rid of all Four Great Diabolic Creeds.” Without even any details on the process, they’ll just hand me the results. That would be a complete failure as the one in charge of intelligence.

To prevent such scenarios, he found it necessary to understand what they did on each trip.

Lu Yang shared, “This time, we simply made the Nine-Netherworlds Creed believe that our Heavenly Court Creed was founded by ancient experts. We also leveraged this opportunity to establish a long-term strategic partnership with them, opening barbeque shops together. We’ll provide the techniques, while they’ll provide the labor. It will be a sixty-forty split of the profits, us taking sixty percent and them forty percent.

“I estimate that after they take some time to figure out the principles of setting up a series of shops, they’ll accelerate the expansion process. I believe they will soon open barbeque chain shops across the continent.”

Dai Bufan expressed high approval of their plan. “That’s actually good news. It looks like the Nine-Netherworlds Creed will stay peaceful for a while.

“By the way, what identity did you give Fifth Elder when you invited him along?” These are tumultuous times; one less problem is one less problem.

Meng Jingzhou answered sincerely, “One of the Heavenly Court Creed’s Nine Great Protectors—the Myriad Treasures Heavenly King.”

Dai Bufan stretched his neck. “Oh, Myriad Treasures Heavenly King. That’s not a bad title. Fifth Elder will like it... Wait, Nine Great Protectors? Where did the Nine Great Protectors come from?”

Lu Yang counted on his fingers. “Eight elders plus Shifu—that makes nine people. We were also thinking of inviting Big Senior Sister to be the creed leader. After all, the Heavenly Court Creed publicly claims to be a colossal power capable of covering the skies with a single hand. Such a lineup shouldn’t be too much, right?”

“So you’re planning to recruit all our sect’s higher-ups into your Heavenly Court Creed?!”

Chapter 336: The Heavenly Court Creed Is Officially Established

“We do have a rough plan like that. Think about it, Senior Brother Dai—if the Heavenly Court Creed only has two ancient geniuses, Meng Jingzhou and me, wouldn’t it seem too empty and unconvincing to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?” Lu Yang explained.

“Even if we include Fifth Elder, having only one Fusion in the almighty Heavenly Court Creed still doesn’t make sense.

“Ultimately, we have to find a few high-level cultivators to support the structure of the Heavenly Court Creed. As you know, I don’t know many people in the cultivation world. After careful calculation, I’ve come to realize that our sect’s elders are the perfect fit for this!”

Meng Jingzhou added, “Besides, things are unfamiliar on the first try but familiar on the second. In the trade of deception, experience is key. The elders have already hoodwinked the Nine-Netherworlds Creed once. Doing it again shouldn’t be difficult.”

Dai Bufan fell silent for a moment, unsure how he should respond—mainly because he found Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s reasoning sound.

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed isn’t foolish. We can’t keep using the same few actors; we’ll eventually need to rotate the cast.

“Alright then. Since that’s the case, go ahead and inform the elders. If they agree, I have no objections.” Dai Bufan was temporarily managing the Great Mission Hall on First Elder’s behalf, but he was still just a disciple and couldn’t decide for the elders.

Though he suspected that the elders would be extremely pleased.

After all, this is a rare opportunity for them to scam the Nine-Netherworlds Creed together again.

Dai Bufan knew that the last time the Dao-Seeking Nine acted together, they nearly caused the Nine-Netherworlds Creed to go bankrupt.

Nine hundred years ago, the elders had originally planned to swindle all of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s money. That way, internal strife would break out, leading to the creed’s collapse.

To their surprise, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was incredibly resilient. Even after losing all their money, they still survived.

~~~

In the Discussion Hall on Heaven’s Gate Peak, eight elders surrounded Li Haoran, as if they were admiring a rare animal. They had just learned that Li Haoran was the reincarnation of the previous Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader.

“To think that reincarnation exists in the world! And it happened right here in our Dao-Seeking Sect? How miraculous!”

“What are you saying? The Dao-Seeking Sect is blessed with outstanding people and sublime ambience. Anything is possible here!”

“I’ve long said that our founding ancestor made the right choice in selecting this location. Our sect’s feng shui is far superior to the other four immortal sects, and I’ve studied feng shui extensively!”

“Big Bro, stop talking. The feng shui you study is all about selecting tombs. I even heard that while you were sleeping in a coffin, you encountered several groups of tomb raiders. They almost died of fright when they saw you, thinking that a corpse had come back to life.”

“Let me correct that. I call this ‘waiting for rabbits by the tree stump.’”[1]

“A golden core that allows limb rebirth and regeneration. It is full and plump, undoubtedly a first-grade golden core. This doesn’t appear to be part of Qin Haoran’s arrangements.”

“I don’t see any problems either. By the way, Junior Nephew Li, do you know what kind of golden core Qin Haoran formed? There’s a possibility that your golden core is connected to his, and he might exploit this to gradually convert you into becoming him.”

Li Haoran ruminated seriously and replied, “I don’t know what Qin Haoran’s golden core was. My impression is limited to just a small memory snippet. Qin Haoran held a Soul-Summoning Banner as he presented his golden core amid the wails of a hundred ghosts and howls of demon beasts. The grand spectacle resembled the parade of a hundred ghost kings.”

With the elders’ vast experience, they soon deduced what kind of golden core it was.

“Based on your description, it sounds like the Wailing Ghosts Howling Wolves Golden Core. The huge commotion can intimidate, perform sonic attacks, and even bolster the grandeur of your entourage when you lack people outside. It has many features.”

Li Haoran was curious. “What grade is this golden core?”

“Second grade.”

“Qin Haoran’s golden core and Junior Nephew Li’s golden cores share no similarities. Junior Nephew Li’s golden core should be fine.”

“Junior Niece Yun Zhi, do you see any issues?”

Yun Zhi, who had been silent all this time, shook her head lightly. “No.”

“There’s no problem then.” The elders concluded the matter.

Just as everyone was about to disperse, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou walked in.

As soon as they stepped into the Discussion Hall, the two felt suffocated; Sixth Elder, who had an Immaculate Immortal Physique, was here. Everyone had been communicating with their spiritual consciousness earlier.

“Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, what brings you two here?” Fifth Elder was puzzled.

Lu Yang transmitted an auditory message with his spiritual consciousness. “Here’s the situation. In order to deceive the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, we specially established a Heavenly Court Creed...” He succinctly described what had happened, with Meng Jingzhou occasionally adding the details.

“And that’s the gist of it. Currently, we’re short on personnel, so we would like to ask all of you elders to impersonate as Protectors of the Heavenly Court Creed.”

Silence. A long silence.

Just when Lu Yang thought the dlers would decline, their spiritual consciousness communication channel erupted into a cacophony.

“There’s such a fun thing? You should have said so earlier! If I’d known, I would’ve gone in place of Old Five!”

“Haoran is my disciple. Of course, I should be the one to go!”

“Junior Nephew Lu is truly full of great ideas. Why didn’t I think of this back then?”

“Heavenly Court Protector—this sounds way more impressive than ‘Dao-Seeking Sect Elder!’”

“Count me in! Count me in! I’m the most adept at deceiving the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.”

“Subduing demons and vanquishing evil is our sacred duty!”

“I missed out on messing with the Everlasting Creed the last time. I can’t miss out on the Nine-Netherworlds Creed this time!”

The elders displayed far more enthusiasm than Lu Yang had imagined. It looked as if they were reminiscing about their youthful days of wreaking havoc a thousand years ago.

“I spend most of my time dealing with tombs, so I shall be called the Nether World Heavenly King.”

“I guard the herb garden and possess deep knowledge of spirit plans. How about the Hundred Herbs Heavenly King?”

“I’m proficient in tempering the body. Even the monks of the Buddhist Kingdom who have mastered the Vajra Body are no match for me. I’ll be the Unbreakable Heavenly King.”

“I’m a Confucian cultivator. I’ll just call myself the Erudite Heavenly King.”

“Lu Yang has already thought of a name for me. It’s the Myriad Treasures Heavenly King.”

“I specialize in concocting pills, and heat control is integral in pill concoction. Why don’t I name myself the Golden Flame Heavenly King?”

“Last time, I was the first to scam the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. Now that we get the chance again, it’s truly fate! I shall be the Fate Origin Heavenly King.”

“Still doesn’t feel quite right.”

It was a lively atmosphere as the elders chattered about their titles. After deciding their own titles, they began concerning themselves with what the Taciturn Daoist Priest should be called.

While the elders debated, Lu Yang silently approached Yun Zhi. She was frowning slightly, as if she was contemplating a major decision.

“Big Senior Sister, are you considering whether to join the Heavenly Court Creed?”

Big Senior Sister’s position as creed leader is pivotal.

Yun Zhi looked up, her eyes sparkling a little. “No, I’m considering what title Shifu should have. Since he’s eloquent and well-versed in debating, what about calling him the Chatter Mouths Heavenly King?”[3]

Chapter 337: I Found You a Franchise Partner

Lu Yang felt that his shifu had great relationships with others. Even while confined in prison, so many people still show concern for him.

Seven senior brothers, one senior sister, and his beloved eldest disciple.

In just a few minutes, Shifu has already acquired several “Heavenly King” titles. How I wish I could deliver this wonderful news to him. He’ll probably be so thrilled that he breaks out of prison just to personally thank his senior brothers and sister for their concern.

As for Big Senior Sister, he probably won’t be thanking her. After all, he can’t beat her.

“I think Shifu himself should decide what 'Heavenly King' title he wants. Big Senior Sister, will you be the creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed?”

Yun Zhi pondered over it and looked at Lu Yang earnestly. “You mentioned earlier that the ruler of the Heavenly Court is Dou Heavenly Sovereign. Is that Senior Immortal Fairy?”

Inside Lu Yang's mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was full of mettle as she stood proudly with her hands on her hips. As the elders were around, it wasn’t convenient for her to show herself, so she transmitted an auditory message to Yun Zhi instead. “That’s right! Bet you couldn’t guess that I’m the ruler of the Heavenly Court! After all, I was the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals. Leading a Heavenly Court is nothing!”

Yun Zhi must never find out about this.

Chapter 338: Confidence From the Unbeatable Golden Core

Unbeatable Golden Core: First-Grade Golden Core.

Chapter 340: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Dilemma

The scripture library of the Dao-Seeking Sect housed more cultivation techniques than the Great Xia Dynasty’s imperial palace. A multitude of cultivation techniques, spanning the ages and written by generations of sect elders, were stored within the scripture library.

Here, Lu Yang also discovered the Pure Yang Cultivation Technique, which Meng Jingzhou practiced.

Compared to Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou had it much easier in terms of cultivation technique. Generations of Single’s Spirit Root predecessors had paved a bright and unobstructed path for him. All he needed was to follow it, and the destination would be the glorious Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

However, Lu Yang didn’t know whether Meng Jingzhou could still tread on this preordained path after breaking the lower limits of his Single’s Spirit Root predecessors and pioneering the Double Single’s Spirit Root.

“Why is it so thin?” Lu Yang was puzzled. The Pure Yang Cultivation Technique I’m holding includes both the cultivation methods of the Golden Core and Nascent Soul Stages. No matter how concise, it can’t be this thin, right?

When he opened the book, only one sentence greeted him.

Jiayou! Don’t lose your virginity. Your cultivation has only just begun!

Lu Yang, “...”

Indeed, many cultivators with a Single’s Spirit Root had reached the Fusion or Transcendent Tribulation Stages. Compared to these two major realms, the Golden Core Stage is merely the starting line.

“So the secret to your Single’s Spirit Root Lineage is just to keep your virginity?”

Lu Yang had heard of a Single’s Spirit Root senior who had reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage after toiling through countless hardships. In celebration, he booked out every brothel in the imperial city and indulged himself for one full month, single-handedly inflating the pricing standards of the capital’s brothels.

The very definition of “revenge spending.”

But those with a Single’s Spirit Root still differed from those in the Buddhist sects.

Buddhist sects emphasized dispelling desires. To them, beautiful women were female skeletons, ultimately turning into a pile of bones; they were ephemeral illusions unworthy of attachment.

On the other hand, those with a Single’s Spirit Root were unable to eradicate such desires. In fact, these desires would intensify along with their advancement in cultivation stage. Faced with such situations, the only recourse was endurance. If they reached a breaking point, they might even start viewing female skeletons as beautiful women.

Lu Yang also stumbled upon an unusual cultivation technique—Body-Sacrificing Spell. As the name implied, it was a cultivation technique that involved sacrificing oneself. It stemmed from the philosophy that all things originated from nature and must ultimately return to nature.

Since everyone originated from nature, why not let oneself return to nature?

Practitioners of this cultivation technique must sacrifice a part of their body in exchange for a boost in cultivation talent and realm. Therefore, these people often became blind, mute, or had their bodies horrifically maimed, with some even reduced to near-empty husks.

Though this cultivation technique was somewhat extreme, it did not yet fall under the diabolic path.

Lu Yang knew of a senior brother who practiced it.

At the Qi Training Stage, he offered his appendix. At the Foundation Establishment Stage, he offered his body fat. At the Golden Core Stage, he offered his hair. At the Nascent Soul Stage, he offered his eyesight. He was now nearsighted and had to wear spectacles.

“All things originate from nature and must ultimately return to nature—what a familiar saying. The Epoch Immortal once said something similar. He told me that all things prosper and decline, and that prosperity and decline are like transient blossoms in the face of nature. Only by emulating nature and returning to the primal state can one attain eternal strength.

“The Epoch Immortal’s words resolved my longstanding question. Imbued with inspiration, I wrote the Everlasting Immortal Art and ascended to an immortal.”

“Immortal Fairy, with how smart you are, what question could have possibly troubled you?”

Though the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was delighted to hear such praise from Lu Yang, she felt that she had to maintain some decorum and appear aloof in front of Lu Yang. I can’t smile so widely just because Lu Yang praised me with a few words.

“Although my talent stands unparalleled throughout the ages, surpassing even the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others, I still encountered challenges concerning immortal ascension.”

Lu Yang nodded. Immortal ascension is key for cultivators. It’s understandable that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy encountered some difficulties in this aspect. “Was it about how to form your Dao Fruit?”

“It was about which Dao Fruit to form.”

Lu Yang, “...” ƒгeewёbnovel.com

“Back then, I had numerous options: the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s 'Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit,' the 'Void Dao Fruit' which was proficient in mysterious spatial wonders, and the 'Time Passage Dao Fruit,' similar to the Epoch Immortal’s. However, I wasn’t satisfied with any of them because they couldn’t showcase my brilliance.

“Based on my progress, I should have been the first to become an immortal, ahead of the Nine-Layers Immortal and the Epoch Immortal. Unfortunately, I struggled when choosing a Dao Fruit because I couldn’t decide which to form.

“And that was how I got delayed just a tiny bit—I swear, it was just a tiny bit!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stressed how short a delay it was by gesturing with her thumb and forefinger pinched together.

Lu Yang had no idea about her definition of “a tiny bit.” Was it a few days, months, or years?

Given the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s claim of being sixteen years old, Lu Yang was distrustful of her concept of time.

“Later, the Nine-Layers Immortal, Epoch Immortal, Heaven Mandate Immortal, and Qilin Immortal ascended one after another, leaving me behind!” Her nose wrinkled in displeasure.

“When the Qilin Immortal ascended, the Epoch Immortal gave me that piece of advice, which sparked my epiphany. Finally, I formed the Everlasting Dao Fruit, which all of them envied!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy exulted in her proud Dao Fruit.

To thank the Epoch Immortal for helping me with my enlightenment, I specifically prepared a feast for him. He was so moved that he wept profusely, muttering something about “regretting his actions.”

He committed the Epoch Immortal’s words to memory and resumed studying cultivation techniques.

In addition to the mainstream cultivation techniques, the scripture library also stored cultivation techniques that slightly deviated from those in the market. These were contributed by the senior disciples. Although they couldn’t create new cultivation techniques, making innovative modifications to existing ones wasn’t a problem for them.

For example, Lu Yang was learning the Great Sun Dharma Body Art. By comprehending the sun and sensing the immense power it contained, one could manifest the “Great Sun Dharma Body” that incinerated everything. When the sun was up, the Great Sun Dharma Body would reach its peak, but after the sun set, the Great Sun Dharma Body’s power would wane.

Hence, a senior female disciple adapted it into the Luna Dharma Body Art. By comprehending the moon, one could manifest the “Luna Dharma Body,” which was as gentle as water and possessed remarkable restorative powers.

More importantly, these two cultivation techniques were compatible, allowing seamless transitions between the Great Sun Dharma Body and the Luna Dharma Body during the day and night respectively.

And this was merely the first level, accessible only to Golden Core and Nascent Soul cultivators. At the second level, one could summon both dharma bodies simultaneously, achieving the 'Shining Sun and Moon' state, thereby doubling their power. At the third level, the two dharma bodies could fuse into one, and the new dharma body “Taiji Transformation Dao” would combine the advantages of both dharma bodies, a balance of offense and defense.

Lu Yang found this cultivation technique extremely terrifying.

On the first floor of the scripture library, he had seen the Sun Observation Art. At the end of the book, it was mentioned that when one reached the Golden Core Stage, they could proceed to the second floor to learn the follow-up cultivation techniques—the Great Sun Dharma Body Art and Luna Dharma Body Art.

At that time, he never anticipated the follow-up cultivation techniques to be so ferocious.

“The senior sister who created this cultivation technique is so impressive! Who is it?”

Lu Yang looked at the author’s name.

Yun Zhi.

He looked up, realizing that he had inadvertently wandered into the legendary “Yun Zhi Section.”

Chapter 341: Creativity Gushes Like A Spring

Lu Yang had long heard about the reputation of the cultivation techniques written by Yun Zhi. After all, the Dao-Seeking Sect had to demarcate a new section dedicated to her works. Unfortunately, he previously only had access to the cultivation techniques on the first floor of the scripture library, which were too elementary.

Today, he finally saw it with his own eyes.

“I knew it! No matter how talented the Dao-Seeking Sect’s disciples are, they can’t possibly produce cultivation techniques of such caliber.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt enlightened. I had thought that the Dao-Seeking Sect’s geniuses were terrifying, with their Luna Dharma Body Art almost rivaling my cultivation technique

Lu Yang pointed out, “What are you saying? Big Senior Sister is also a disciple of our sect.” While the most outstanding disciples in Big Senior Sister’s cohort, like Senior Dai and Senior Brother Ji, were trying to catch up with the elders, she had long left them in the dust.

So this is disparity.

The shelves before them were lined with an assortment of cultivation techniques, either modifications of existing cultivation techniques or her new creations.

“Hehe, overwhelmed by the number of cultivation techniques Yun Zhi has written?” A weathered chuckle rang in Lu Yang’s ears.

Turning around, Lu Yang discovered a hunched elderly man beside him, unremarkable at first glance.

“Just an idle old man minding the scripture library to pass the time. You can just call me Old Tao.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy immediately jumped off her bed, eager for the tale.

“When your shifu first brought Yun Zhi here, she was still not that tall, probably at this height.” Old Tao gestured toward his chest level. Although he was hunched and short to begin with, young Yun Zhi had barely reached that height.

“She was reticent and cold, though I didn’t know whether it was her personality or a result of her growing up in a secret domain. However, after she came to the scripture library, her expressions became more vivid.

“Her whole face spelled upset. She pouted, claiming that these cultivation techniques were poorly written. When I asked her for the specifics, she simply shook her head like a pellet drum.[1] She said she couldn’t tell but insisted that it was poorly written.

“Although these cultivation techniques had flaws, they were far beyond what a little girl could discern. I laughed it off, assuming that the little lass was pretending to criticize the cultivation techniques because she found them too hard to understand.

“Who could have imagined? It hasn’t been that long, yet that lass has already advanced to a level no one else can catch up to, with even her own unique insights into cultivation techniques.” Old Tao lamented. I totally didn’t expect that little girl back then to have become so powerful now.

“Cultivate properly, and perhaps you might surpass Yun Zhi one day!” Old Tao patted Lu Yang’s shoulder, placing a huge responsibility on him.

“Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art.

“A cultivation technique hidden in a cave domain from the past.

“Cultivators usually possess far longer lifespans than mortals, seeking eternal life through cultivation. However, this cultivation technique goes against the grain, burning one’s lifespan to break through their cultivation realms and rapidly increase their cultivation. In critical moments, one can also temporarily burn their lifespan to boost their combat power.

“The Great Mission Hall mandates that every disciple complete two missions annually. In combat, through forcibly burning other people’s lifespans, one could make the other party obtain tremendous power and age rapidly. Before the other party can unleash their newly obtained power, they would have died from aging.

Lu Yang could feel his scalp prickle. The day I surpass Big Senior Sister is when pigs fly.

But the good news is that Big Senior Sister didn’t write these cultivation techniques when she was at the Golden Core Stage.

I still have a chance.

Lu Yang stopped thinking about the external world, gradually immersing himself in the various cultivation techniques, including Yun Zhi’s, the elders', and mainstream ones circulating in the market. He began analyzing each creator’s mindset and their intent behind each step. He was so absorbed that he was lost in a trance, forgetting everything else.

In a flash, half a month had passed. Lu Yang woke up from those myriad cultivation techniques and suddenly remembered his original purpose in coming here was to continue writing his cultivation technique.

“Let’s start writing!”

Lu Yang scratched the back of his head. Having read numerous cultivation techniques, his mind was brimming with knowledge, and he was confident he had great prospects on the path of cultivation techniques. However, when he picked up a brush and tried to begin writing, he realized he had no idea how to start.

“I clearly understood everything when I was reading, though...”

Lu Yang braced himself to start writing, with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy not uttering a single word as she watched him by the side. Reminding him now will harm him instead.

After brainstorming for ages, inspiration finally struck him, and he picked up his brush again to write his own cultivation technique.

“Just like this!” Creativity gushed like a spring as his brush flew across the paper like dragons and snakes.

Half a month of reading cultivation techniques didn’t go to waste. He felt like he had internalized everything and could even innovate by building upon existing foundations. An endless stream of ideas was transferred onto the paper.

“Yes, this is how the next part should be written!” His only frustration now was that his brush moved too slowly to capture the whirlwind of ideas in his mind.

Two days later, the Golden Core Chapter of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra was completed. Through multiple rounds of revisions, he had made the cultivation technique more polished and sharpened the language. freewёbn૦νeɭ.com

Chapter 342: Big Improvement

Upon hearing that Yun Zhi had approved twenty percent of his painstakingly written work, Lu Yang was genuinely pleased. It’s rare to earn any approval from Big Senior Sister. Even if it’s only twenty percent, it’s valuable progress. This is a good start.

It’s much better than the complete rejection the last time.

That half a month of forgetting to sleep and eat while studying assiduously in the scripture library, combined with two days of wracking my brain to write so much, wasn’t in vain.

Twenty percent this time, forty percent next time—in no time, I’ll be able to write a cultivation technique that matches Big Senior Sister’s level.

The future looks bright!

With that, the Immortal Sect Tournament concluded with a severely wounded Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“Your understanding of cultivation techniques is still superficial, making you inevitably imitate other people’s cultivation techniques, whose understanding is also superficial. They assume they understand everything, but their understanding is actually incomplete.

The positive and negative effects cancel each other out.

Only a fool enters a fight they know they’ll lose.

Chapter 343: A New Use for Illusions

With Big Senior Sister around at Heaven’s Gate Peak, how could there be any danger?

She looks so innocent. Who would have thought she’d come up with something only men think of?

I’m counting on this to make money.

Chapter 344: Eighth Elder

Lu Yang reckoned that if Tao Yaoye were to defect to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, the creed leader would probably enshrine her as their holy main or even directly hand over the position of creed leader to her.

This money-making method is far more lucrative than Qin Haoran’s loan schemes. It isn’t even an exaggeration to call it “profit without capital.” No investment means no risk of losses.

Furthermore, there’s no need to hire actors or reshoot scenes dozens of times. Illusions can be randomly conjured without restrictions. The special effects are also practically indistinguishable from reality.

If one dies in an illusion during battle, it would mean real death—such is the realism of illusions.

As for the storyline, there’s nothing to worry about. The daily happenings in the cultivation world can serve as inspiration. With a bit of refinement, they can be adapted into films, while the longer plots can become serialized dramas.

We have a material at hand—Shifu’s pingshu story, Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect, can be the source material for a film.

Though it’s true that when the Taciturn Daoist Priest first entered the sect, Eighth Elder had raised him, laying a solid foundation for him to grow astray in the future.

Though it’s true that nine hundred years ago, Eighth Elder scammed the Nine-Netherworlds Creed of all their money and drove its creed leader then into committing suicide.

Lu Yang was filled with newfound respect. I didn’t expect Eighth Elder’s deception skills to be this brilliant! To think that he has never been caught! Shifu can’t compare to this!

After all, Shifu is a ruthless person who could trick the Minister of Justice into landing in prison. Even with an optimistic estimate, Shifu probably hasn’t been released from prison yet.

Lu Yang heard that ever since the Minister of Justice was locked up in Dayan Commandery’s prison, the entire Ministry of Justice had relocated there for official business, leading to unprecedented clear skies and order in the commandery. Not a single crime occurred.

The bad guys weren’t stupid. With the entire Ministry of Justice stationed in Dayan Commandery, only someone with a death wish would commit crimes right under their nose.

After all, they were not the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

However, there were also downsides. Meng Jingzhou shared that the officials in the capital city resorted to taking leave just to have a tour of Dayan Commandery’s prison for the novelty of it.

They also justified it as “showing concern for colleagues.”

While they were at it, they would also casually suggest to the Minister of Justice to sentence the Taciturn Daoist Priest to the death penalty.

Sixth Elder rolled her eyes at Eighth Elder. Having been his senior sister for two thousand years, she knew him best.

“Yes, you were never caught—you would always turn yourself in, claiming it could reduce your sentence.

The Great Xia Penal Code stipulated that crimes that had exceeded the statute of limitations would no longer be subject to prosecution.

Chapter 345: Even Big Senior Sister Is Not My Match!

Normally, diabolic cultivators avoid the authorities like the plague.

Sixth Elder didn’t dwell too long on this topic. “Enough. I’m not here to discuss who you had scammed. We need your help with something related to talismans.”

Tao Yaoye shot Lu Yang an innocent look, which the latter understood immediately. See? You can’t blame me for associating Eighth Elder with swindling. The moment we met, he himself admitted that he scams people.

Such quick-witted minds are suited to be under my tutelage.

He also knew that Lu Yang was quick-witted, but he dared not poach anyone from Yun Zhi.

Overpowering illusions could leave mortals disoriented even after they broke free from the illusions, leaving them unable to distinguish between illusion and reality.

The fellow daoists who could discuss talismans with Eighth Elder were naturally top-tier experts in talismans themselves.

One would need to infuse the Three Treasures into the crevices of the template all at once.

Gingerly approaching the foot of Heaven’s Gate Peak, Lu Yang verified that the puppet wasn’t waiting for him at the entrance before ascending with a peace of mind. Arriving at the summit, he saw Yun Zhi quietly sitting at the stone table and enjoying the tea. The incredibly docile puppet was pouring tea for Yun Zhi, a stark contrast to its usual attitude toward Lu Yang.

A brand new cultivation technique lay on the stone table. It was precisely the Golden Core Chapter of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra.

“Try cultivating with it. I’ve made revisions to some parts based on your original work.”

Lu Yang looked like he had gained a priceless treasure. As expected of Big Senior Sister—far more reliable than the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy constantly pesters me about teaching me the Play-Dead Technique, unlike Big Senior Sister, who writes cultivation techniques for me.

The handwriting reflected Yun Zhi’s character—neat, pretty, and icy.

Since the cultivation technique was written based on Lu Yang’s thinking framework, he grasped its contents quickly. After poring over it twice, he had already committed it to memory and was ready to circulate energy through his Cosmic Loops.

Following the theories, Lu Yang concentrated his consciousness into a single strand of spirit qi, guiding it to circulate within his body in a regular pattern.

Soon, he completed a Macrocosmic Loop, marking his successful initiation into the cultivation technique.

Hubris swelled within Lu Yang. “I’m truly a rare genius through the ages. I’m the strongest in existence!” He felt that cultivation was as effortless as breathing and that no one could compare to his talent.

His gaze drifted to Yun Zhi, who was serenely sipping her tea.

Even Big Senior Sister is not my match!

“Wait, that’s not right!” No matter how dull his senses were, he still noticed that something was wrong with him.

How suicidal I must be to entertain such illogical notions like “Even Big Senior Sister is not my match!”

It’s the Unbeatable Golden Core! It has imbued me with the confidence of being unbeatable, but I could usually suppress such thoughts with logic. However, the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra has amplified its effects, making me believe I’m unbeatable in the world!

Lu Yang couldn’t stop his body from charging toward Yun Zhi. The Unbeatable Golden Core was even blaring warnings to refrain from such actions.

“PLEASE COMMIT SUICIDE IMMEDIATELY TO MAINTAIN A 100% WIN RATE.

“PLEASE COMMIT SUICIDE IMMEDIATELY TO MAINTAIN A 100% WIN RATE.”

The Unbeatable Golden Core blabbered endlessly to request that Lu Yang maintain its guaranteed victory rate.

Yun Zhi lifted her eyelid, realizing that she had overlooked this unique characteristic of the Unbeatable Golden Core when writing this cultivation technique.

Fortunately, Lu Yang had seen his fair share of storms and adversity, reacting swiftly in this critical moment.

“Scatter Dou-Beans For Soldiers!”

He forcibly transferred control of his body to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who was watching the spectacle.

“Eh? Eh??”

Color drained from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face. I was just watching the spectacle. Why have I become the spectacle myself?

Controlling Lu Yang’s uncontrollable body, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy attacked Yun Zhi and was sent flying through the air with a finger.

Lu Yang successfully upheld his unblemished track record of being undefeated.

Chapter 346: Qing Province Grand Ceremony

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was sent flying from a flick of Yun Zhi’s finger and ended up hanging upside down on a nearby tree branch, her body swaying to and fro.

“Lu Yang, you’re disrespecting immortals!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was furious. I was innocently dragged into this. This calamity was completely undeserved.

In my prime during the ancient era when I commanded the winds and clouds, who dared to treat me like this?

Lu Yang replied respectfully, “It’s not that I was disrespecting you, Immortal Fairy. It’s simply because I have just formed my golden core, so I’m not yet familiar with it. I was hoping you could demonstrate the proper usage of the Unbeatable Golden Core just now.

“Thanks to your demonstration, I now know how to use the Unbeatable Golden Core.”

“Really?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy eyed Lu Yang suspiciously. She couldn’t shake off the feeling that something was amiss.

“I am but a mere mortal. How could I dare deceive you, Immortal Fairy?”

“True.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt she was magnanimous and decided to let the matter slide.

The puppet jumped to pick Lu Yang down from the branch, holding him by the collar like he was a misbehaving kitten.

Yun Zhi placed two fingers on Lu Yang’s wrist like a physician taking his pulse. She nodded almost imperceptibly. “So that’s how it is. This was my oversight. When I was writing the cultivation technique, I forgot about the Unbeatable Golden Core’s unique trait of instilling you with blind confidence. The cultivation technique amplified your confidence, robbing you of rational thought and bodily autonomy.”

She retrieved the fallen cultivation technique from the ground. It spontaneously ignited and turned to ashes, as if it had never existed. “I’ll make more revisions. Wait for a while.”

Yun Zhi sat beside the stone table and sliced open space, taking out an empty book. After some brief contemplation, she figured out how to modify it, and her brush began flying across the pages.

Before long, a new version of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra’s Golden Core Chapter was completed.

“Come. Test it out again.”

Lu Yang accepted the cultivation technique. Compared to the previous version, only select phrases had been altered. Can these minor changes really suppress the Unbeatable Golden Core’s impulses?

Lu Yang circulated energy through his Macrocosmic Loop again and stole a glance at Yun Zhi, who sat with her eyes closed in a relaxed manner.

He exhaled in relief. I have no suicidal urge to beat Big Senior Sister this time.

Lu Yang settled into the lotus position right there and sensed the changes brought about by the cultivation technique.

The biggest change was the brightness and clarity in his heart. The cultivation technique had illuminated his path, and he simply had to follow it.

Previously, his cultivation depended on piling up power without true improvement in his cultivation realm. However, with this new cultivation technique, his accumulated power came in useful, elevating him from the Basic Golden Core Stage to the Basic Golden Core Stage.

It might seem like he had made no progress, but there were some changes, though minimal.

On the other hand, his spiritual consciousness had expanded slightly, which also enlarged his mental space. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s bed was originally placed against the wall—the very boundary of the mental space—but now, her bed was two handspans away from it.

Noticing the change, she pushed her bed back against the edge. She preferred sitting with her back against the bed and feet against the wall, finding this posture comfortable.

“Is Lu Yang around?” Meng Jingzhou called out in a hushed voice.

Given his usual boisterous personality, he would always be hollering whenever he looked for someone. However, this is Heaven’s Gate Peak—home to Lu Yang and the terrifying Big Senior Sister. Even with eight times the courage, Meng Jingzhou wouldn’t dare to raise his voice here.

“Big Senior Sister, you’re here?” Meng Jingzhou bowed obsequiously upon spotting Yun Zhi leaning against a tree with her eyes closed.

Yun Zhi acknowledged him softly. She was alerted the moment Meng Jingzhou had stepped into Heaven’s Gate Peak. “Why are you looking for me?”

Meng Jingzhou said mysteriously, “It’s good news, of course! Have you heard of the Qing Province Grand Ceremony? It’s about to begin!”

Lu Yang’s knowledge of the common events in the Great Xia Dynasty was limited. “What is the Qing Province Grand Ceremony?”

“It’s a grand ceremony for cultivators, spearheaded by the Qing Province’s authorities in collaboration with a few first-class sects. Held every year at the start of the eighth month, it features a range of festivities, including duels and auctions. The main purpose of this bustling event is to attract young cultivators to stay in Qing Province, so participants are mostly around our age.”

Lu Yang’s eyes sparkled. I rarely get to interact with peers of a similar age. This is a good opportunity.

“Let’s go! By the way, is the Qing Province you’re talking about the same one Fifth Elder mentioned—where twenty thousand years ago, the Transcendent Tribulation Qing Province’s governor moved the neighboring city to the province under the pretense of a duel?”

“That’s the one.”

Yun Zhi opened her eyes slowly, revealing a trace of curiosity. “Fifth Elder told you about the Qing Province’s governor?”

“Big Senior Sister, you know about it too?”

“Of course. After all, that governor was our sect founder.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

For some reason, the two were not surprised.

It does match the Dao-Seeking Sect’s style—perfectly logical yet utterly absurd.

“Keep the matter of the Qing Province’s governor to yourselves. Spreading it would tarnish the Dao-Seeking Sect’s reputation.” As the de facto leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, she valued the sect’s prestige and reputation.

Though she had no idea how the outside world perceived the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Meng Jingzhou asked with curiosity, “Big Senior Sister, what became of that governor in the end?”

“Later, he developed Qing Province methodically. The Qing Province Grand Ceremony was his brainchild. It attracted numerous talented cultivators, achieving remarkable results, which drew other provincial governors to emulate. Under his administration, the Qing Province flourished. After attaining fame and success, he retired and returned to the sect.”

Lu Yang realized an issue. “Hold on, members of the Five Great Immortal Sects can serve as officials in the imperial court?” He had assumed that the Great Xia Dynasty would bar members of the Five Great Immortal Sects from holding office out of fear and suspicion stemming from the sects’ high statuses.

“Of course, they can.”

Meng Jingzhou began to enumerate a few examples. “The court is hungry for talents and sages. And where better to find them than the Five Great Immortal Sects? They even offered the abbot of the Hanging Monastery the position of prime minister! But he simply declined it.

“And the sect leader of the Prison Suppression Sect was also invited, but he turned it down.

“For promising young talents like you and me, the court would welcome us as officials. However, unlike the abbot of the Hanging Monastery, we have to pass the imperial examination.”

Yun Zhi reminded, “Lu Yang, you’re ineligible for the imperial examination or any official post.”

Lu Yang was flabbergasted. “Why?” I have no plans of becoming an official, but I can’t possibly not even have an opportunity to do so, right?

“It’s because of our shifu.”

Realization dawned upon Lu Yang. With his intelligence, he figured it out immediately. Twenty thousand years ago, the Dao-Seeking Sect was still not the leader of the Five Great Immortal Sects. However, the sect is no longer the same as it was. It is now the undisputed number one immortal sect.

The imperial court is worried about the Dao-Seeking Sect becoming the sole dominant power, so they dare not let the sect’s disciples, or perhaps, direct disciples of the sect leader like me, become officials. This would avoid the collusion between the sect and society, thereby threatening the stability of the Great Xia Dynasty’s ruling position.

Yun Zhi continued, “Our shifu has committed multiple offenses. His disciples and our grand-shifu are forbidden from holding any official positions.”

Chapter 347: Where’s My Royalty Fee?

Yun Zhi produced a gilded invitation whose cover revealed its lavishness. “The Qing Province Grand Ceremony includes a fighting tournament for the younger generation. As someone who thrived in lively environments, it was naturally the more the merrier for him.

Only after Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had departed did Yun Zhi suddenly remember something and open the invitation.

On the 3rd day of the 99,860th year of the Great Xia’s calendar, the Qing Province Grand Ceremony will commence as customary. We humbly request your esteemed sect to send outstanding disciples to participate and offer some guidance as judges.

“Back home, I often heard stories about these grand ceremonies and how spectacular they were. Just listening to the descriptions made me wish I could check it out myself. Unfortunately, I hadn’t started cultivating then, so I wasn’t qualified to attend the grand ceremony.

These mid- and high-level cultivators were fairly older than Lu Yang and his peers. If they were present, the younger generation would inevitably feel restrained and dare not act freely.

Lu Yang understood this all too well. It’s like when classmates come over to play. The vibes when the parents are present versus when absent are totally different.

Once they entered Qing Province’s territory, the old horse withdrew its spatial-traversal abilities. Since they took small, remote mountain paths, no one was around to see them. However, they were now in Qing Province, which was crowded and bustling; it could terrify pedestrians.

Meng Jingzhou stuck his head out, grinning at the nearby scenery. “We’re almost there.”

Lu Yang peeked out his head from the other side. Dense mountain forests, lush vegetation, and massive peaks stretched before them, dotted with limestone structures in a picturesque fashion. It was as if the scene came straight out of a painting.

Although these structures were said to be hastily constructed, their architecture was exquisite, clearly crafted with attentiveness. Numerous cultivators that looked like tiny black dots in the distance darted between the structures.

Whoosh!

Meng Jingzhou turned to glance at Lu Yang, whose expression had turned peculiar.

I did invent this flying carriage, but after Fifth Elder had Li Haoran apply for a patent, this matter had slipped my mind. It’s already at the mass-production stage?

“Wait a minute, where’s my royalty fee?”

Chapter 348: Spending Money to Avert Calamity

Even if only a small group of people produced flying carriages, the royalty fees Lu Yang received could still make him insanely rich.

Previously, Lu Yang had assumed that the patent was still under review and that mass production of the flying carriage had yet to begin, so he pushed the matter to the back of his mind.

But now, the flying carriage was blatantly soaring away. There’s no way the patent hadn’t been approved.

Could it be that Fifth Elder has a kind face but an evil heart, embezzling my royalties?

The thought flickered through his mind, but he immediately dismissed it.

Fifth Elder wouldn’t stoop to coveting such petty profits.

Whatever. I’ll just ask Fifth Elder when I see him. Lu Yang shelved the issue.

~~~

The old horse pulled the carriage to the foot of the mountain, where a newly built inn stood. Since the Qing Province Grand Ceremony would last seven days, they couldn’t let cultivators camp out in the open and weather the elements for so long. It would be unbecoming of Qing Province.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had arrived early, so rooms were still available.

“Give us two of your best rooms!”

“Sure! Two Heaven-Grade guest rooms. May I ask if you would also require a guest room for your horse?”

Meng Jingzhou was taken aback. Could this person have seen through my old horse’s unfathomable power and decided to treat it as a person?

The innkeeper smiled. “Guest, let me explain. Our inn offers complimentary spirit beast care services, but due to space limitations, spirit beasts are housed in the backyard. During the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, many experts would bring their high-level spirit beasts along, and keeping them together in the backyard may inevitably affect the other spirit beasts to some extent.

“If you don’t mind potential disturbances to your spirit beasts, we are also happy to look after yours at no cost.”

Meng Jingzhou considered the offer. Although I don’t know the old horse’s exact strength, a guardian that my family has assigned me should have a pretty high cultivation realm. It’s more likely to bully others than get bullied.

But then again, given the old horse’s penchant for seducing little mares, it’ll be more appropriate to give it a private room.

“Then give the old horse its own room too.”

“Aye! Three Heaven-Grade rooms!”

“Old horse,” Meng Jingzhou whispered, “Secretly share the truth with me—what exactly is your cultivation realm? I guarantee that I’ll pretend I never heard it.”

The old horse cast a sidelong glance at Meng Jingzhou and snorted twice, clearly not buying Meng Jingzhou’s nonsense.

After Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou headed upstairs, another group arrived, though they appeared far less affluent than Meng Jingzhou.

“Innkeeper, three Mortal-Grade rooms.”

“Apologies, dear guest, but we don’t offer Mortal-Grade rooms.”

“The Mortal-Grade rooms are already booked out?” the man exclaimed. He mentally counted his funds. Just enough. “Two Earth-Grade rooms then.” With a bit of squeezing, we can make do with two rooms.

“Apologies, dear guest, we only have Heaven-Grade rooms available.”

“What?!” We are just Qi Training cultivators. How could we possibly afford such luxurious rooms?

“Senior Brother, let’s try another inn.”

The innkeeper chuckled. “Pardon my frankness, but other inns also only have Heaven-Grade rooms available.”

Their faces darkened. It’s only the first day, and we already have to sleep on the streets?

The innkeeper was accustomed to seeing such reactions. “It’s not what you think, dear guests. Every year, when the Grand Ceremony commences, brawls over Heaven-Grade rooms break out. To prevent such disputes, the Qing Province’s authorities instructed us to upgrade all guest rooms to Heaven-Grade rooms while charging the same price as Mortal-Grade rooms, with the authorities subsidizing the difference.”

Rather than letting chaotic cultivator brawls disrupt public order, the Qing Province authorities were more willing to spend extra spirit stones to nip any potential risks in the bud.

~~~

Meng Jingzhou was oblivious to the low price of his “Heaven-Grade room.” He never had any concept of such trivial money.

“Lu Yang, let’s go out and explore when you’re ready! I heard there’s a street up the mountain selling antiques and magical treasures.”

“Gotcha.”

“What?”

To win Senior Sister’s favor, the star atlas is a must!

Chapter 350: Antiquity Secrets

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sighed plaintively, lamenting the mournful state of the era. “Why is your era filled with rumors and slanders? Even immortals aren’t spared.”

As a member of this era, Lu Yang listened to her teachings solemnly and expressed that he would engage in deep retrospection.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked, “The Heaven Mandate Immortal was such a great person. Although he was unlucky that I fought him when challenging those above my level, he was still a rare genius and shone in his own right. Who would have thought that after becoming an immortal and attaining fame and success, he would fall victim to the rumors of later generations?”

Lu Yang seized the opportunity to ask, “Did the Heaven Mandate Immortal have a wife or children?”

“Probably not. But he was quite popular with women.”

“How so?”

“By the standards of ordinary people, the Heaven Mandate Immortal was exceptionally handsome, though I never felt the same way. Of course, it could be because I always left him bruised and battered.

“Before he ascended to an immortal, powerful female cultivators who admired him would often abduct him, forcing themselves on him. It wasn’t just once or twice. I personally witnessed it at least five times, and based on the rumors, it occurred many more times than that.”

“...How enviable—ah, no, I mean, how unfortunate.”

Lu Yang continued to flip through Antiquity Secrets and noted that while the book mentioned the Four Ancient Immortals, only the Heaven Mandate Immortal was referred to by name. The others were labeled with vague descriptions, such as “the Demon Immortal” and “a certain immortal.”

“Either the Heaven Mandate Immortal was the most famous of the Four Ancient Immortals, or a book that can be bought for three thousand spirit stones won’t reveal much.”

Considering that the Heaven Mandate Immortal had created the Lightning Tribulation, Lu Yang had reason to suspect that the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s name was widely circulated among high-level cultivators, or rather, widely spurned.

“Look here! It mentions the great battle between the ancient Dragon and Phoenix ancestors, where the old Phoenix ancestor unleashed “Rebirth from Fire!” Meng Jingzhou pointed to one of the pages, excited about seeing a familiar story.

He had heard the tale from the pure-blooded phoenix in Luofeng Commandery, whose version was more detailed. Nevertheless, the broad strokes aligned.

“This individual had a penchant for harems and thrills, so he defeated every last hundun in his tribe, turning them all into women. And since the Hundun Tribe could alter their appearances at will, they were all dazzling beauties.
